British Industrial Mission Visits Manchuria for Investigation 53

Claims It Has Nothing to Do with Politics

(London) The Morning Post today published a letter from Lord Barnby, the leader of the British industrial mission to Manchuria, stating that the country's visit to Manchuria has nothing to do with political issues. The letter mentioned a report that quoted a statement he made, saying that according to a London representative of a certain Japanese newspaper, he had expressed his opinions on the political relations between Britain, Japan, and Manchuria. He felt that there must be some misunderstanding, because the mission he led to Japan and Manchuria has nothing to do with political issues, and political issues are not within the scope of the investigation at all. Moreover, he himself is not qualified to express opinions on political issues involving relations between Great Britain and other countries. He felt obliged to clarify in order to avoid misunderstandings about the purpose of the mission to the Far East. The mission to the Far East is purely non-official in nature and aims to promote commerce and hope that business figures on both sides will make friendly contact. According to reports, the delegation has four representatives from the British business community and is scheduled to depart from London tomorrow to "Manchukuo" to investigate everything and find out whether the British business community can cooperate with the local business community to seek publication. In addition to visiting Manchuria and Japan, the delegation members seem to take the opportunity to visit several commercial centers in China. (24th Reuters)

International Currency War 55

Britain Uses Equalization Fund to Maintain Gold Pound

1.5 Million Pounds Have Been Used

The United States Still Has a Large Amount of Gold Transported to Europe

(Washington) The United States still has a large amount of gold being transported to Europe today. Experts are wondering what the outcome will be. New York bankers claim that $1,060,000 in gold will be transported to Europe immediately. If the government does not change its silver policy, then gold exports will increase sharply. People generally suspect whether the Treasury Department will be forced to raise the price of gold or continue to sell gold at a price of $35 per ounce when the dollar falls again, thereby profiting. Most financiers still believe that the government is trying its best to maintain the status quo. Treasury officials are now closely monitoring the flow of international currencies, especially rumors about foreign exchange and their impact on the dollar. The Treasury Department still denies that a currency war will occur with Britain. News from London today said that the British Equalization Fund purchased millions of pounds in gold. The Federal Reserve Board in Washington announced today that gold holdings increased by $4 million this week, and the reserve for gold certificates increased by $2 million, which proves that the Treasury Department's gold reserves are balanced. (24th Kuo Min News Agency)

(London) The recent decline of the pound compared to the firmness of the dollar shows that Britain and the United States are now pursuing their own currency policies, which are diverging. The continued decline of the pound is a force that lowers prices and is still at work, such as the outflow of British funds. Some pessimism exists, not only limited to the pound, but also because of the possibility that the United States' reduction in currency value, although denied by Treasury Secretary Morgenthau, may be doubtful whether the current price of the dollar can be maintained if the currency value is indeed reduced. The general opinion here is that the weakness of the pound is due to the sale of gold pounds by continental Europe, coupled with the fact that British banks have recently transferred funds to Paris, because French short-term bond yields are more favorable. New York's export of gold has stabilized the price of the dollar today, but the future of the dollar is not without concern. This is why continental Europe is selling. British authorities used the exchange equalization fund yesterday to maintain the gold pound. The number is different, some said 1 million pounds, some said 3 million pounds, but according to the most reliable news, about 1.5 million pounds were used. (25th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) The British-French exchange rate fell to 75 francs 73 today, while the closing price yesterday was 76 francs 03. Today's price has created a new low. Britain is expected to take active measures to maintain this price and wait for it to continue to fall. The dollar price yesterday was 14.93, which is relatively stable today. (25th Reuters Telegram)

(London) The Times today published an editorial, admonishing the continuous outflow of silver from China, saying that after the US government passed the Silver Purchase Act in May, in addition to nationalizing the domestic silver, it also purchased silver in large quantities abroad, causing the price of silver to rise and undermining China's ability to sell its goods overseas. The United States' relationship with silver is far less important than China's. China should have the right to speak in plans to raise silver prices in order to control it, which is in line with reason. If the economic disorder reaches the point of forcing China to abandon the silver standard or forcing it to adopt strict austerity, it would not only be a great misfortune for China, but also a great misfortune for Western exporters. (25th Reuters Telegram)

The United States Agrees 56

To Extend the Naval Conference for Two Years

Negotiations Are of No Use Now

(Washington) Responsible officials here stated today that the State Department supports extending the naval conference for two years. The current situation does not allow the conclusion of a new treaty, so extending the London Naval Treaty for two years may solve the naval problem. However, responsible officials deny that this matter was initiated by London. Official declarations say that it is impossible to achieve any agreement next year, given the tense political situation in Europe and Asia, and extending the naval conference will give major naval powers time to reach a better understanding with each other and then decide on specific naval policies. The current goal of naval powers is to increase rather than reduce naval strength. Japan's demand for equality, Britain's demand for building 22 more cruisers, and the active shipbuilding of the United States, Italy, and France are three new developments that will undermine the success of the 1935 conference. Extending the Washington and London Treaties for two years or until 1940 is not difficult, but Japan may declare that it will abandon the current treaty, which will see global naval competition break through historical records. (24th Kuo Min News Agency)

Roosevelt 57

Advocates the Development of the Shipping Industry

In Addition to Economic Use, It Also Has National Defense Uses

(Washington) President Roosevelt declared today that the United States plans to develop the shipping industry and make it an integral part of the entire economic lifeline of the United States. The government will never abandon American shipping rights to foreigners. Recently, Agriculture Secretary Wallace criticized the government's shipping industry relief policy. President Roosevelt's statement is a response to this criticism. The President said that Wallace's argument only involved one-sided economic reasons and forgot that there were other reasons, such as national defense, which are even more important. The United States has a need to consolidate the shipping industry, for the following reasons: (1) National defense; (2) The United States is not involved in the war during wartime; (3) Preventing foreign mail shipping companies from raising water feet. Harryman, president of the American Chamber of Commerce, is also a supporter of the shipping industry, saying that the shipping industry is now extremely declining, and any further hindrance will have unimaginable consequences. (24th Kuo Min News Agency)

Reorganizing Old Debt Issues 58

US-Russia Negotiations Fail

(Washington) The State Department admitted today that negotiations between Soviet Russia and the United States regarding the $768,500,000 debt have reached a stalemate. After receiving a counter-proposal on the debt issue from Soviet Russian Ambassador to the United States, Troyanovsky, the State Department immediately informed reporters that an agreement was unlikely. The US-Russia debt negotiations had moved from Washington to Moscow, and then from Moscow back to Washington, but no progress was made. This debt consists of foreign bonds issued by the Tsarist and Kerensky governments, which the Soviet Russian government refuses to acknowledge. Furthermore, the Soviet Russian government seized American property worth $440,000,000 after taking power, and this issue is also being negotiated together. The reason the State Department is reluctant to admit that the negotiations have broken down is that leaders in the business community deeply hope that the restoration of diplomatic relations between Soviet Russia and the United States will expand trade between the two countries. (National Telegram, 24th)

European Customs Conference 64

Soviet Russia Actively Develops the Arctic 65

(National News Agency, Moscow, 25th) In the first half of this year, the Soviet Russian authorities dispatched more than sixty icebreakers and other vessels to explore the Arctic Ocean. More than thirty vessels are still in the Arctic, proving that the Soviet Russian authorities are sparing no effort to develop the Arctic region. The Soviet Russian Arctic exploration team uses Arkhangelsk as a base, transporting various exploration tools to the White Sea from there. Airplanes and automobiles, totaling 7,500 tons, are stationed at each station. Government officials stationed in the Joseph Land area study scientific work for periods ranging from three to five years. It is now planned to send another 200 Soviet Russian scholars to Gwadar.

(TASS, Arkhangelsk, July 25th) The Northern Sea Route Administration's Arctic exploration team is now aboard the icebreaker "Rusanov," departing from here to carry out organizational work at the Nordvik oil field. Super-grade kerosene was discovered there in 1932. The first oil pool will be excavated this year. Housing, an airfield, a motor vehicle depot, and an airplane hangar will be built near the oil field.

Japanese Set Up 66

Radio Station in Changchun

(Beiping) Changchun News: The Japanese are setting up a radio station in Changchun, decided to be 100 kilowatts. The Kuanchengzi broadcasting station is currently assembling parts and is scheduled to begin broadcasting on November 1st. If a Hiaton receiver is used, radio waves from all over Japan and all of China can be received. This move by the Japanese is purely to engage in a broadcasting war with our country's radio stations. If its wavelength is the same as any of our radio stations, then that radio station will be affected. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Dongbao Discusses the Franco-Soviet Pact 89

Containing Japan and Italy

The Turmoil in the Far East

Led to the Two Countries Agreeing

According to a report in the Tokyo Hochi Shimbun on the 18th, after the conclusion of the Locarno Treaty in Eastern Europe, the Franco-Soviet alliance, which has close ties, has also been completed. Among the countries of Eastern Europe, with a spirit of mutual assistance, Germany is isolated in Western Europe. At the same time, in order to resist Japan in the East, Russia has joined the alliance. Therefore, at the League of Nations General Assembly in September, Russia will be one of the permanent council members. If so, the complex international relations in Europe will have a great impact on the Far East. However, it is incomprehensible that informed people in Japan regard this as commonplace. The occurrence of this matter, although originating in Europe itself, must also be said to be due to the turbulent international relations in the Far East, which have contributed to it. The politicians in Moscow, in the partnership of Russia and France, all have the concept of "the terror of Japan and Germany." The urgency of today's Russian war is deeply reflected in the minds of Europeans, which is truly unfortunate. Russia, situated between Japan and Germany, must have prior preparations. Even if Germany is not currently taking action, Russia must also defend the Far East in order to preserve the borders of Europe in the event of an emergency. Since Hitler took power, Russia has felt particularly uneasy about the West. However, why are France and the Little Entente countries so eager to approach Russia? One reason is that Stalin and Litvinov's practical policies have restored the trust of Western Europe, and another reason is that Germany's current situation is almost the same as that of Russia and France. (Omission) Therefore, Russia's revival of the pre-war Franco-Russian alliance is a measure of self-defense. However, from the French perspective, the Franco-Russian alliance was originally a defense against Germany, but it inevitably has the intention of containing Japan. Today, French public opinion on Japan is the same as that of Britain, divided into two factions. The right-wing sympathizes with Japan, while the center and left-wing supporters of the alliance oppose Japan. Russia is vigorously promoting Japan's aggressive ambitions in order to stir up world public opinion. Therefore, it is clear that the current Franco-Russian rapprochement is increasingly unfavorable to Japan.

Gubeikou Sub-Customs 90

Starts Inspecting Goods and Levying Taxes

Foreign Goods and Cereals are Major Imports

Luan-Yu District Sub-Customs Not Yet Established

According to Ping News, the Gubeikou Sub-Customs officially opened at 8:00 AM on the 22nd. No ceremony was held. First, the flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun was raised, followed by the hanging of the wooden sign "Tianjin Customs District Great Wall Line Gubeikou Sub-Customs." Then, work began, and import goods were inspected and taxed. After the establishment of the Gubeikou Sub-Customs, Northeastern goods imported into the interior through various ports of the Great Wall will be exempted from taxation in accordance with the provisions of Section 3 of the Interim Measures for Tax Collection. The items include perilla seeds, watermelon seeds, cottonseeds, hemp seeds, wheat, oats, millet, sorghum rice, and glutinous millet, other various grains, wheat flour, fodder, oil cake, horse hides, horsehair, sheepskins, camel hair, animal bones, coal, etc. According to a telephone report received today (August 23) by the Beiping office of the Tianjin Customs Great Wall Sub-Customs, imports have been dominated by foreign goods and cereals in recent days, and taxation has begun. Furthermore, Gao Yuanji, the Director of the East Sea Customs, led the heads of the four sub-customs in the Luan-Yu District from Beiping to Luanzhou some days ago. As of today, Gao's report has not yet been received. The office expects that the establishment date of the four sub-customs will be delayed until early September at the earliest due to transportation obstacles. (23rd)

Decree from Chiang to the Hubei Provincial Government 91

Detailed Reports on Disaster Conditions in Various Counties

Hungry People Flock to the Wuhan Provincial Government, Requesting Urgent Relief

Affected Counties Divided into Three Grades for Relief Based on Severity

Hankou Dispatch: The Hubei Province suffers from severe drought and flood disasters, with no harvest from fields and a shortage of grain. The disaster victims in various counties, including Huang'an, Macheng, Huangmei, Guangji, Qichun, and Huanggang in eastern Hubei, and Daye, Yangxin, Puqi, Xianning, Chongyang, and Wuchang in southern Hubei, are facing dire straits. Initially, they abandoned their homes and committed suicide due to famine. Subsequently, they resorted to seizing and robbing grain. Now, they are gathering crowds to commit violence, leading to tragic incidents. Those closer to the provincial capital have mostly come to seek food. Both Wuhan areas are experiencing overcrowding. A few days ago, more than 1,000 disaster victims from Puqi came to the provincial capital, petitioning the provincial government, the civil affairs department, and the relief association. Their miserable condition was unbearable to witness. The authorities, concerned with public order, have already taken measures to disperse them. On the 23rd, the provincial government telegraphed the Central Relief Commission again, requesting urgent relief. The telegram stated, "Respected members of the Nanjing Relief Commission, your esteemed telegram is acknowledged. The register of disaster areas and the relief plan are being prepared promptly by the Civil Affairs Department in conjunction with the Relief Association. However, the disaster situation in Hubei Province is worsening daily. Hungry people are flocking to Wuhan, and the provincial government is struggling to provide urgent relief and dispersal, which is beyond its capacity. Moreover, in areas affected by bandits, it is particularly important to seek immediate pacification to prevent the spread of unrest. It is proposed to allocate a certain amount of urgent relief funds to address the immediate crisis. We anxiously await your response. Respectfully, the Hubei Provincial Government." The Disaster Relief and Famine Preparedness Committee believes that the method of relief should be differentiated based on the severity and urgency throughout the affected areas. Therefore, the affected counties have been divided into three grades. Generally, Puqi, Huangmei, Guangji, Huanggang, and other counties are classified as first-grade disaster areas. Qianjiang, Mianyang, and other counties are classified as second-grade disaster areas. Jianshi, Shishou, and other counties are classified as third-grade disaster areas. Relief will be distributed according to these grades. Meanwhile, personnel will be dispatched to Sichuan, Anhui, Jiangxi, Henan, and other provinces to purchase rice and grain and conduct large-scale price stabilization measures. The provincial government has also ordered all counties to release the accumulated grain in their granaries for price stabilization to maintain stability. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is deeply concerned about the disaster situation in Hubei Province. In addition to repeatedly telegraphing the Central Government to coordinate relief efforts, he has also telegraphed the Hubei Provincial Government to compile a comprehensive report on the details of the disaster and submit it for review. The telegram stated, "Since the beginning of summer this year, the weather has been severely dry, and the autumn harvest in rural areas is hopeless. Reports of disasters from various provinces have been pouring in. Looking ahead, there is cause for deep concern. In addition to the disaster relief and drought prevention plan of your province and the effective plans for implementation, which have been telegraphed separately for detailed reporting to seek active relief, a precise investigation of the actual disaster situation in your province is necessary as a basis for a comprehensive plan. The affected area of each county, the severity of the disaster, the quantity of grain lost, the number of affected households, whether there are storage facilities in the disaster area, and whether there are alternative grains available nearby should all be thoroughly investigated and compiled into a comprehensive report to be submitted for review within a time limit. The columns in the table should comply with the previous order and should not be exaggerated or falsely reported, which would mislead the situation." (23rd)

Four Breaches at Changyuan 92

The Liu Embankment Completed Successively

Over Three Hundred Villages in Hua County Flooded

Precarious Situation Upstream in Zhongmu

Kaifeng Dispatch: He Youliang, an engineer from the Yellow River Conservancy Commission stationed at the Hebei River Affairs Bureau to assist in flood prevention, telegraphed Commission Chairman Li Yizhi today, reporting on the situation of the breaches at Changyuan. He stated that the Liu Embankment at the original 25th and 21st openings was completed on the evening of the 18th. The Liu Embankment at the original 8th and 17th openings was completed on the evening of the 20th. The Liu Embankment at the original 25th opening is 172 meters long, the original 21st is 120 meters long, the original 8th is 230 meters long, and the original 17th is 210 meters long. The silt accumulation on each Liu Embankment is quite effective. Efforts are currently being made to extract soil and rush to close the openings. The Henan Provincial Party Affairs Commissioner's Office also telegraphed the Central Government today, requesting it to forward the telegram to the National Government, instructing the Executive Yuan to urgently order the Hebei Provincial Government to close the breaches and to quickly allocate large sums of money for the urgent relief of disaster victims in Yu (Henan) and Hua counties who have been flooded. The original telegram stated, "The Changyuan levee of the Yellow River in Hebei Province was breached last year due to lack of defense, inundating houses and causing extreme misery. The affected area has not yet recovered its vitality. This year, the flood season has arrived, and no precautions were taken in advance, resulting in the same mistake. The old breaches that were closed last year between Shitou Village and Dacheji have successively collapsed again. Dozens of villages outside Changyuan City have suffered another catastrophe, and more than 200 villages in Hua County, Henan Province, have also been affected. The disaster situation is very serious. Moreover, the flood season has not yet passed. If another flood occurs, the impact on the levees on the north bank of the Yellow River in Henan will be even more worrying. According to various sources, the collapse of the levee this time was indeed due to insufficient manpower and delayed rescue efforts. In addition, the soil quality of the new levee was sandy and lacked mud, and the gullies and wave troughs were not filled firmly. The levee protection project was also not constructed, and the levee foundation was not strong. There were no sheds built on the north and south sides of the levee for the laborers to be responsible for guarding. Once the flood season arrives, they will be submerged. The river affairs authorities and engineering personnel of the province have failed to perform their duties effectively and cannot shirk their responsibility. We believe that the state has spent a huge amount of money to assign specialists to handle river defense, but they have not been able to do everything within their power, resulting in another catastrophe. How can the common people bear this again? We have heard that the Executive Yuan has ordered the Hebei Provincial Government and the Yellow River Conservancy Commission to investigate and severely punish the responsible personnel, which is sufficient to clarify rewards and punishments and appease public grievances. As for the disaster area, families have been ruined and are crying out for food. Urgent relief and post-disaster recovery are of utmost importance. Therefore, we urgently telegraph, requesting that the National Government be immediately informed and instruct the Executive Yuan to order the Hebei Provincial Government to find a way to close the collapsed openings before the arrival of the main flood to avoid future troubles. At the same time, allocate large sums of money quickly to provide urgent relief to save the disaster victims. We cannot express our urgent hopes enough. The Henan Provincial Party Affairs Commissioner's Office, worship print."

A telegram from Mazhen, Shanzhou (21st) stated that the Yellow River water level had risen sharply again by one meter and fifty-nine centimeters. At noon, it rose another two centimeters. Chen Ruzhen, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, immediately telegraphed each sub-bureau to be vigilant and ordered the director of the Shangnanliu Sub-bureau to personally go to the old course of the Yellow River in Lanfeng and the civilian embankments in Kaocheng to supervise the construction and guard. Chen himself, together with Tao Jizheng, rushed from Liuyuankou to Rongze Flood Control Station to inspect the river. The dikes were all solid, and the projects could be guaranteed to be safe. However, the sixth dam of the Eight Forts upstream in Zhongmu was directly impacted by the main current, with the head of the dam collapsing by one zhang and five chi and the tail collapsing by two zhang. The newly purchased stones had not yet arrived, and the situation was relatively dangerous. The director of the Shangnansu Sub-bureau was immediately ordered to quickly transfer nearby stored stones for emergency relief. It is currently being protected by throwing stones, and it is expected to stabilize in a few days. (22nd)

Guangdong Province 93

Planning the Construction of the Guangzhou-Shantou Railway

The Entire Line is Over 430 Li Long

Construction Cost is 40 Million Yuan

The Entire Route is Scheduled to be Completed in Five Years

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Guangdong Provincial Government planned to build the Guangzhou-Shantou Railway (from Guangzhou to Shantou) before the Lunar New Year. Starting from Shahe in Guangzhou, the route passes through Boluo, Huiyang, Renshanxu, Haifeng, Lufeng, Huilai, Puning, Jieyang, and reaches Shantou. Then, it connects with the Chaoshan Railway in Shantou to reach Chao'an. The entire line is over 430 li long. The construction cost and the cost of acquiring the completed Chaoshan Railway and returning the capital to its shareholders amount to 38,174,000 yuan. In addition, there are other unexpected expenses of 1,826,000 yuan, totaling 40 million yuan. The entire route is scheduled to be completed in five years. The first year is for surveying and preparation. The second year is for acquiring land and building the earthwork roadbed. The third year is for completing the construction of the roadbed, bridges, and culverts, after which the track laying will begin. The fourth year is for building the locomotive factory, stations, and tracks, and the line will begin to operate. The fifth year is for completing all unfinished work and clearing the debts of the Chaoshan Railway. As for the fundraising methods, the Preparatory Committee will be reorganized into a Fundraising and Management Committee. The government will allocate 40% of the funds, and the remaining 60% will be raised from the public. The Fundraising Committee will be jointly organized by representatives from the Provincial Government, the Department of Construction, the Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce, the Chaoshan Railway Company, and the eight counties along the route, including Boluo, Huiyang, Haifeng, Lufeng, Huilai, Puning, Jieyang, and Chao'an. They will be responsible for fundraising and supervising the construction. The preliminary survey of the route has been completed by the technicians and survey teams dispatched by the Department of Construction last month, according to the above-mentioned route, and a preliminary map has been drawn. This work has recently been completed, and the preliminary map and the survey process have been reported to the Department of Construction and the Provincial Government for review. On the 17th of this month, the Provincial Government submitted it to the Provincial Affairs Conference for discussion and decided to have the Department of Construction conduct a second survey to facilitate construction. After receiving the order, the Department of Construction is now preparing to send another survey team and technicians to start the second detailed survey, which is scheduled to be completed within three months. It is planned to complete the surveying and mapping matters by the end of this year, and the land acquisition and earthwork construction will begin next year. (August 19)

Sichuan Province 94

Mountain Torrents Cause a Strange Disaster

The Tuo and Min River Basins are the Most Severely Affected

Chengdu Dispatch: Although Sichuan is mostly mountainous, it also has many rivers. The name Sichuan is derived from the four major rivers, the Jinsha River (the long main river), the Min River, the Tuo River, and the Jialing River, which flow through the province. They are all formed by the confluence of hundreds of streams, originating from deep mountains and remote valleys, with steep terrain. Once mountain torrents erupt, they cannot be discharged in time, often causing floods. Since the beginning of summer this year, continuous rain has plagued various places, causing the riverine areas to suffer a strange disaster unprecedented in a century. The bandit suppression areas, such as Suixuan, Wanyuan, Guangyuan, and Nanjiang counties, and the non-bandit areas, such as Shiqi, Guanghan, Pengxian, Xinfan, and Wenjiang counties, have been the most severely affected. The true extent of their losses has been确实 ascertained. It is still unknown how many other places have not been fully investigated or have suffered lighter disasters or have recently been flooded. The basins of the Tuo River and Min River are particularly affected, as their tributaries are numerous, the terrain is relatively flat, and accumulated water is more difficult to drain. Liu Xiang and the Pacification Committee here believe that Sichuan's bandit troubles are not yet over, and this strange disaster has struck again, leaving it riddled with holes and unable to save itself. They have telegraphed Chairman Lin, Chairman Chiang, Premier Wang, Minister Kong, and the National Relief Commission, requesting them to consider the plight of the Sichuan people and allocate large sums of money for relief. Two telegrams have been obtained, and their original texts are disclosed below:

(Telegram Requesting Relief) (Titles Omitted) Esteemed officials, I have learned that since the beginning of summer this year, continuous rain has fallen in Sichuan Province, and mountain torrents have suddenly erupted. The Min, Tuo, Jia, and Ya rivers have successively flooded, inundating vast areas. According to reports from various counties, those near the mountains include Dazhou, Xuanhan, Wanyuan, Guangyuan, Wenchuan, Anxian, Danling, Jiajiang, Hongya, Emei, Ebian, Gongxian, Pingshan, and Changning counties. Those along the rivers include Dayi, Qionglai, Pujiang, Xinjin, Shuangliu, Leshan, Qianwei, Pengshan, Ziyang, Santai, and Deyang counties. In addition, the counties near Chengdu, which have always relied on the Dujiangyan irrigation system, have also suffered flooding due to excessive rainfall. The water level at Baopingkou has risen to around 23 lines. The stone weirs for diverting water from the two rivers have been washed away, causing Guanan, Pixian, Wenjiang, Xinfan, Chongning, Pengxian, Guanghan, Shifang, and Jintang counties to suffer flooding. People's fields and houses have been destroyed, and their belongings have been washed away. The living are exposed to the elements and hungry, unable to guarantee their survival. The dead are floating in the water, unable to be buried. The entire land is filled with mournful cries, and the situation is extremely tragic. The most severely affected areas include Lijia Nian in Shifang County, Jiuchi Pu in Pengxian County, the fourth district of Wenjiang County, and Huangdan Chang in Pingshan County. The entire population, livestock, and houses in the town have been washed away by the floods, and few residents have escaped. This is a major disaster unprecedented in decades. In addition, Guangyuan has also been hit by hailstorms, while Qijiang, Youyang, Xiushan, Qianjiang, and Cangxi counties have suffered prolonged droughts, causing the crops to wither and die, and they have reported drought disasters, with no hope for the autumn harvest. The water and drought disasters in the above counties all urgently require relief. I am lacking in ability to provide comfort and am deeply responsible. I have separately instructed local civil and military officials, legal entities, and respected elders to rush to provide urgent relief and ordered the counties affected by the floods to rush to protect and defend, and to do their best. I have not dared to bother you with a request for relief. However, Sichuan suffered a drought disaster last year, and the efforts to provide urgent relief have exhausted all resources. This year, water and drought have occurred simultaneously, and the disaster area is vast. At this time, the suppression of the bandits is urgent, and military needs are enormous, causing financial strain. It is difficult to continue. Seeing the misery of the displaced, it is indeed beyond my power to rescue. I believe that you, esteemed officials, have the people's suffering at heart and are looked up to by all. News reports that the Executive Yuan has telegraphed all provinces affected by disasters to investigate and report the disaster situation in detail, and I know that you have long been concerned about the disaster in Sichuan. I humbly request that you order the Ministry of Finance to allocate large sums of money and send personnel to Sichuan to investigate and distribute aid to rescue the disaster victims. I anxiously await your orders. I am only submitting a preliminary report of the disaster situation. Once the reports from all counties along the river are complete, I will submit a detailed supplementary report. In addition to separate telegrams to the Ministry of Interior and the National Relief Association, I am sending this telegram for your consideration."

(Telegram from the Pacification Committee) (Titles Omitted) Esteemed officials, the suffering of the people of Sichuan is deep. Both crop pests and disasters have struck, leaving the land full of scars. The banditry has lasted for years, and the suppression has not yet been fully completed. The water and drought disasters have successively been reported. According to investigations, the counties along the Qu River in eastern Sichuan, such as Suiding, Hanxuan, and Wanyuan, have recently suffered repeated floods. Li Shaoqian, the magistrate of Dazhou County, telegraphed that the county had suffered continuous heavy rain and flooding. The Qu River, from Luojiangkou to Mutoushi, a distance of over 200 li, had flooded, drowning over 100 people. Countless houses, livestock, fields, crops, and miscellaneous grains had been washed away. In the three districts outside the east, south, and west city walls, a total of five li in length, the houses and goods of the residents in the streets were all washed away. The total number of disaster victims in the county reached 3,000 families, with property losses exceeding 500,000 yuan. According to an investigation report from Xuanhan, the towns of Fan Kuai, Tuhuangba, and Huajianba in the county all suffered heavy flooding, resulting in huge losses. Zheng Guowu, the magistrate of Wanyuan County, telegraphed that the county had suffered two floods in the past month, and houses and livestock along the river had mostly been washed away. The cultivated land had been destroyed. The people in the recently recovered areas had suffered another disaster, and their livelihoods were on the verge of collapse. In northern Sichuan, the Jialing River rose sharply last month, and the magnitude of the flood was unprecedented in previous years, causing great losses in various places along the river. In particular, Guangyuan and Nanjiang suffered hailstorms in addition to mountain torrents, and the situation was extremely serious. The above areas had just experienced banditry and were now hit by floods. The survivors of the disaster were on the verge of extinction. We must earnestly request that you show sympathy for the people who have suffered multiple disasters and quickly allocate funds for relief. As for the non-bandit suppression areas, such as Shifang in western Sichuan, mountain torrents suddenly erupted in the middle of the night, and the river water rose sharply by several zhang, causing a violent flood. The affected area stretched for over 100 li and was over 10 li wide. More than 10,000 households were affected, with over 5,000 deaths. Over 10,000 people were homeless, with no possessions left. In Deyang, the river water rose sharply by three or four zhang in the middle of the night, causing the banks to collapse and the dikes to break. The water flowed in all directions, destroying over 3,000 houses and submerging nearly half of the county's fields. Over 3,000 people were drowned. In Guanghan, the large and small rivers rose simultaneously, and 80% of the rural towns became a swamp. The loss of submerged crops, livestock, destroyed houses, and land was difficult to count. In Peng County, floods spread along the river, submerging over 10,000 mu of fields and washing away over 1,300 houses. Over 900 people were drowned in Jiuchi Pu and Mengyang Town due to the sudden flood in the middle of the night. Over 130 people were drowned in other places along the river, and countless cattle, pigs, and sheep were lost. In Xinfan, mountain torrents erupted, and the fields, bridges, houses, and livestock along the river were mostly washed away and submerged, and over 200 men, women, and children were drowned. In Wenjiang, many of the bridges and dikes were destroyed, and the damaged crops and washed-away livestock were countless. In Heba Town, over 180 people were drowned due to the sudden flood in the middle of the night, as people were unable to escape. In southern Sichuan, Qionglai was hit by mountain torrents in the night, with the water level rising by two zhang. The houses of residents along the river were washed away by 600 or 700 families, and over 2,000 people were drowned. The amount of submerged fields and crops cannot be counted. In Pingshan, mountain torrents erupted in the night, and the river water rose sharply, washing away all the fields and crops along the river. All 300 or so houses in Huangdan Town were completely washed away, and over 300 people were drowned. In Gongxian, heavy rains fell for days, and mountain torrents erupted, causing the water level in the plains to rise by several feet, damaging fields, mountain soil, and houses, and causing countless damage to crops. The residents along the river were particularly affected, and many people and livestock were drowned. The above descriptions only mention the counties that have been most severely affected, and they are based on reports from local officials and gentry or investigations by members of this committee. They are all reliable and not fabricated. This is a strange disaster unprecedented in a century, which is heartbreaking and frightening. Although the authority of this committee is to pacify the bandit suppression areas, the banditry is not yet over, and natural disasters have struck again. If we want to prevent the banditry from spreading further, we must ensure the overall stability of Sichuan, but the people of Sichuan are impoverished and exhausted, and they are trapped in extreme poverty and unable to save themselves. Therefore, we humbly request that you show sympathy for the people of Sichuan and allocate large sums of money to provide relief to the people in the counties that have been most severely affected by this disaster, to rescue the starving and drowning, and to stabilize the region. We are extremely grateful. Zhang Lan, Chairman of the Sichuan Bandit Suppression Area Pacification Committee, bowing seal."

Nanhui 95

Bandits Conspire to Rob a Night Boat

The night boat from Zhoupu has always traveled between Zhoupu and Nancheng, carrying goods and money for various merchants and passengers, and it has never had any problems. However, last night, as the boat was returning from the city to Zhoupu and passing through Yaolu in Lidong Township, the seventh district northwest of Sanzao Town, more than ten li away from the county seat, suddenly a person on a small boat collided with it. Four passengers on the boat immediately drew out their pistols, threatened everyone to remain silent, and robbed all the belongings of the ten or so passengers on the boat. The boat owner, Feng Binggen, who was carrying a total of over 370 yuan in remittances from various merchants (Pinyin He et al.), was also completely robbed. They all got on the small boat and sped away. The total loss is estimated to be over 500 yuan. It is rumored that the bandits had learned that the merchants had entrusted the boat with a large amount of money, so they conspired to rob it.

Songjiang 96

The Embezzlement Case of Grain Tribute

Director Niu Orders County Magistrate Jin

The embezzlement case of grain tribute in the East Ward of this county, involving the conversion of fields and the misappropriation of provincial education funds, amounts to no less than 20,000 yuan. When the case was discovered, Director Niu of the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office ordered the county to investigate and respond. The day before, County Magistrate Jin reported that Director Ye had concealed tax revenue and deserved punishment, so he had been placed under supervision and strict recovery efforts were underway. It is now known that Director Niu issued an order to County Magistrate Jin on the 22nd of this month, the full text of which is as follows: "Your report has been read and is being reviewed. According to a report from Supervisor Wu Baohuang, the investigation table of provincial education funds under the field tax item for each year filled out by the county shows a decrease compared to the actual tribute amounts for each autumn tax reported by previous finance bureau directors. The uncollected amounts for each year have also been reduced by over 10,000 shi of grain. The land price tax of the 22nd year, excluding the grain tribute, is certainly related to the embezzlement case of grain tribute in the East Ward. By checking the investigation table and the autumn tax amounts reported by previous directors, it can be seen that the reduced grain tribute is over 10,000 shi, and the suppressed grain tribute is over 4,000 shi. In fact, over 3,000 shi of grain tribute in the East Ward of Pubei has already been fully paid by each landowner. The 7,000 shi of grain tribute in the East Ward of Punan has also not been completely resisted by each landowner. Director Ye concealed the facts and submitted a vague report. The county government should consult the grain tribute atlas and recall the grain tribute seals to solemnly announce the reduction of the grain tribute amount and prevent embezzlement. The county magistrate's response to each item was not examined in advance and continued to shirk responsibility afterward. Director Ye is undoubtedly guilty, but can the county government shirk its responsibility? The case is important and should be thoroughly investigated. How can it be dismissed with a mere empty gesture of strict recovery efforts? According to the previous report, you should immediately comply and promptly submit a clear list of the protected land area and mu in the North and South Pubei field conversion grain tribute, and truthfully report why the autumn tribute amount filled in the investigation table does not match the amount reported by previous directors, whether the converted field grain tribute in South Ward is over 10,000 shi, and whether there was no income from the grain tribute in the 18th, 19th, 20th, and 21st years, to facilitate review. As for the newly appointed Director Yang, regarding all tax revenue, the store guarantee bond volume should be quickly copied and sent to this office for review. Do not delay, and this order is urgent."

Verdict on Case of Using Counterfeit Currency 97

In the middle of this month, Zhou Desan, Zhu Buxiang, and Wang Yongji, who were wearing uniforms and resembled military officers, suddenly came to Qibao Town and used counterfeit currency in various shops. Afterward, the shops noticed and reported to the Huazhuang Sub-station, which intercepted them. The shopkeepers who were victims were summoned for questioning. Zhou Desan and others pleaded guilty and were sent to the County Court. After investigation by the Prosecutor's Office, the facts were clarified, and a public prosecution was filed. After repeated trials, the verdict was announced on the 25th. Zhou Desan and Zhu Buxiang were each fined 200 yuan for using counterfeit currency, and Wang Yongji was acquitted.

Zhenze Farmers Gather in Large Numbers and Cause Trouble 100

Farmers from Zhenze County, under the jurisdiction of this county, once looted rice and cakes last month. The local police tried to dissuade them, but were met with resistance, and many were injured by thrown tiles. A subsequent investigation revealed losses exceeding seven thousand yuan. Later, the county government dispatched a security team, and the farmers fled upon hearing the news. Currently, various sectors are requesting: (1) a thorough investigation to apprehend the ringleaders and bring them to justice; (2) that the district office and the district chamber of commerce continue to hold relief meetings, raise funds, and actively prepare a rice-lending bureau; (3) that the county security team, together with local police and militia, provide separate defenses.

After the new indica rice came onto the market, rice prices stabilized slightly. However, due to the prolonged drought and dry riverbeds, prices are again expected to rise. Wuxi 104

Preventing Locust Plague Amidst Drought Disaster

This year, the weather has been arid and dry, and the crops have withered, allowing locust nymphs to take the opportunity to invade the fields in the countryside, and they are often seen. Recently, the county government received a report from Zhao Hongbin, the district head of the sixth district, that locust nymphs were found in the area, damaging the rice crops. After receiving the report, Magistrate Yan, regarding the matter of preventing and controlling the locust plague, repeatedly received detailed instructions from provincial orders. If immediate measures are not taken to eliminate them, they will inevitably spread, causing endless harm. However, deeply concerned that the district heads may not pay enough attention, he specifically copied and distributed the Jiangsu Province's reward and punishment regulations for pest control personnel to the district heads yesterday, and telegraphed them to instruct the township chiefs to pay attention to prevention and control, and to report in detail whether there were any locust plagues in their areas.

Liyang Refugees Come to Wuxi to Beg for Relief 105

The drought in southern Jiangsu Province is severe, and the disaster situation is serious. Since the beginning of autumn, there has been no rainfall, the crops have withered, there are no measures to draw water, and people's drinking water has become difficult. Although the disaster situation in Wuxi has not reached the most serious level, the rivers are also drying up, which is worrying. In recent days, a large number of famine refugees have been found near Gongyun Bridge and outside the West Gate, supporting the old and carrying the young, resting on the road. According to an investigation by our reporter, these refugees are mostly from Liyang. Because the crops in their hometown were hopeless, they wandered to Wuxi, without food or clothing, and their situation was very miserable. According to the refugees, since May 20th of this year, the entire county has only received five or six minutes of rain, and the land is red for thousands of miles, and most of the crops are hopeless. Robberies of rice have occurred from time to time. A farmer surnamed Gu from Dongxiang, with a family of six, men and women, who usually cultivated more than ten acres of land, committed suicide by poison with his entire family on the morning of the day before, because there was no grain in the house and no way to borrow. Furthermore, two brothers surnamed Di from Chengxi, each with more than 300 acres of fertile land, who were very generous in helping the poor and assisting the needy, distributed all the rice they had stored in their homes last month for relief, but it was just a drop in the bucket and did not solve the problem. Recently, the villagers went to request again, but the Di brothers could not cope and hanged themselves. Furthermore, Shi Amao, a villager from Chengbei, with a family of ten, had run out of food and could not survive, so he bought one yuan's worth of arsenic and all died in the middle of the night. Furthermore, the Liyang Infant Asylum has recently taken in many girls. Wang, a farmer from Shezhu, brought his wife to Liyang and put up a sign and sold his five-year-old son along the street. Later, Huang bought him for five yuan, and Wang used the five yuan to buy rice and returned home, separating flesh and blood. There were also two young women, each with three children, all young, who wanted to go out to make a living, abandoned their children, and left home, etc. Those who heard it were all saddened. In recent days, thousands of Liyang refugees have come to Wuxi on foot along the Xiyi Road, braving the summer heat. Fortunately, the villages they passed through did not harass them.

Important Proposals for the County Administration Conference 106

The Wuxi County Government is scheduled to convene a county administrative conference on September 1st. Qian Sunqing, the director of the county assets office, has submitted three proposals, which have a chain relationship with the local finances of various counties and are extremely important. The topics are recorded as follows: (1) The county administrative conference should definitely adopt the local budget and final accounts as the central task, and hold meetings once before the start and after the end of each accounting year, in order to make public administration and facilitate local understanding. (2) County local funds should definitely be used locally in principle. If there are provincial offices that need to be operated locally, the purpose should also be clearly stated, and it must be related to the local area before it can be included in the budget, in order to clarify the boundaries and avoid confusion. (3) The drought is severe, the disaster is serious, and the social economy is unprecedented. The government should promptly concentrate manpower and financial resources to provide disaster relief and prepare for famine as the central task of the local government, and other construction projects that are not related to people's livelihoods should be stopped as appropriate to alleviate the people's strength and avoid heavy hardship. Furthermore, Yang Hanxi, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, also proposed to pre-plan work-relief measures to relieve the famine, which is also extremely important due to the heavy drought and disaster.

For more than ten years, the business flourished and made a lot of profits. Commentary

Inside Story of the German June 30th Incident 115

— Wuwei

= Division of Left and Right Wing Forces =

= A Glimpse of the Left Wing's Conspiracy =

Although Chinese newspapers and magazines have discussed the German June 30th incident extensively, the inside story remains a great enigma. After reading recent British and American magazines, the author has gained some insights and will describe them below for the reference of those concerned about international issues.

In simple terms, the German coup was a movement by the left wing of the National Socialist Party to seize power. Unexpectedly, Hitler was well-informed and preemptively struck, and the movement failed. Hitler's quick-witted action has won the admiration of those who worship heroes. In fact, the open and secret struggles between the left and right wings of the German National Socialist Party have not been limited to a single day. The ambitions of the left wing have been exposed from time to time, and the right wing has been attentive to dealing with them. Otherwise, Hitler's response to this incident would not have been so agile.

Hitler's plan to prevent the left wing from rebelling was already in the making in the spring of this year. One example is that at the 14th anniversary celebration of the National Socialist Party on February 25th, Hitler asked one million party members to re-swear their absolute loyalty to him personally. From this point of view, Hitler had already foreseen the left-wing division movement within the National Socialist Party. Therefore, in order to prevent problems before they occur, he took the action of asking party members to reaffirm their oath. The second point is that Hitler ordered Goering in March to organize 200,000 secret police, ostensibly to prevent conspiracies outside the party, but in fact to prevent rebellions within the party. These secret police, or as servants, or as doormen, or as post office clerks, or as telephone operators, in various forms, were all available. Therefore, once there was an alarm, Hitler would know. The safe suppression of this incident also depended entirely on these secret police. It can be seen that Hitler's defense against the left-wing rebellion was already well-planned.

Hitler's expectation was to make Germany a country without parties or factions. Although the revolution of the National Socialist Party had eliminated the enemy parties, it had not changed the social organization. The social hierarchy was no different from other capitalist countries. Due to the different interests of the classes, there were different political views, and due to the different political views, left- and right-leaning movements were formed. These signs can be seen in two aspects: (1) the figures in the Hitler government, and (2) the group forces. The government figures belonging to the right wing are Foreign Minister Neurath, Finance Minister Krosigk, National Bank Governor Schacht, and Minister of Economic Affairs Schmitt. Before Hitler came to power, his attitude was unbiased, but in the past year, he has gradually leaned to the right. As of today, it is safe to include him in this group. Those belonging to the left wing are Minister of Education Rust, Minister without Portfolio and leader of the Guard Troop Roehm, and Minister of Food Walter Dame. In addition, Minister of the Interior Frick, who was neither left nor right before, has now turned to the right.

As for the group forces, the division is as follows: There are currently six types of group forces in Germany: (1) the National Defense Army, (2) the police, (3) the secret police, (4) the Black Shirts, (5) the Steel Helmet League, and (6) the Storm Troopers. Of these six groups, the first five are all right-wing forces, while the Storm Troopers have a large number of left-leaning members, so they can be regarded as left-wing forces. Let's describe their strength separately. Although the National Defense Army has only 100,000 people, the length of service is as long as twelve years, so the training they receive is the most sufficient in Europe. In addition, the number of people is small, and the equipment is excellent, so in terms of combat effectiveness, they are much better than the soldiers of other European countries. Before Hindenburg's death, this group often followed Hindenburg's will. Hindenburg himself often took a detached attitude towards politics, so the National Defense Army did not participate in many coups. However, in the final analysis, it is the backbone of the right wing. As for the German police, there are 150,000 people. Although the Treaty of Versailles stipulates that they should not receive combat training, it is an open secret that they have received combat training. Prussia accounts for the majority of these police. Goering, in his capacity as the Minister of the Interior of Prussia, has the power to command the Prussian police, so this force can be said to be entirely in the hands of Hitler and Goering, becoming a force of the right wing. Not to mention the 200,000 secret police organized by Goering. As for the Black Shirts, they are Hitler's specially selected loyal followers from the Storm Troopers. Although the number is only a few thousand, they are Hitler's most trusted team. As for the Steel Helmet League, it was originally an organization of veterans. Before Hitler came to power, there were one million people. Initially, Hugenberg was the leader, but now it is the soda industry entrepreneur Fraz Seldte. After Hitler took office as Prime Minister, he contacted and specially appointed Selde as Minister of Labor. Although the people in this group have experienced the Great War, they are all middle-aged, so their thinking is very stable, which is very different from those who are young and frivolous. Therefore, it is also a major force of the right wing. Finally, the Storm Troopers were created by Hitler himself. The members are mostly young people with youthful spirits. Demonstrations and slogans are their specialty. Before Hitler came to power, they fought with the Communist Party. After taking office, they attacked the organs of the Communist Party, mostly by the power of the Storm Troopers. Since the Hitler Party gained power in March of last year, the Communist Party and the Socialist Party have been suppressed by Hitler, and many have changed their party affiliation and joined them. The purpose was to make the Storm Troopers lean to the left, so as to achieve their goals. Before the June 30th incident, the number of people in this group had increased to 2.5 million. Although their combat capabilities are far below the National Defense Army and the police, their strength cannot be ignored due to their large number.

Now that the six major groups have been clarified, it is not difficult to see the inside story of this incident. Since the class hierarchy has not been changed under Hitler's rule, the left- and right-leaning of political figures and political groups is inevitable. Since the various group forces have different left and right, conflicts are inevitable. Since this spring, these conflicts have been common. One is the conflict between the Storm Troopers and the Steel Helmet League, and the other is the conflict between the Storm Troopers and the National Defense Army. The initiator is indeed Roehm, the leader of the Storm Troopers. Roehm saw that the members of the Storm Troopers were increasingly leaning to the left, and he wanted to use this trend to replace Hitler. In order to achieve this goal, he naturally started by annexing the Steel Helmet League and the National Defense Army, which were regarded as the strongholds of the right wing. In March of this year, Roehm carried out his plan to annex the Steel Helmet League. He first requested Hitler to order the Steel Helmet League to be incorporated into the Storm Troopers of the National Socialist Party based on the principle of a non-party, non-faction, and nationally integrated nation. Hitler thought that he could expand his power, so he was happy to accept it. However, due to the resistance of the right wing, he adopted a compromise method, changing the name of the Steel Helmet League to the United Corps of Veterans of the National Socialist Party. It was nominally the National Socialist Party, but in fact it still existed independently. Since then, the Storm Troopers and the Steel Helmet League have been at odds with each other, and conflicts have occurred frequently. On June 11th, after the leader of the Steel Helmet League, the current Minister of Labor Selde, gave a speech to the Steel Helmet League, the car he was riding in was stoned and madly insulted by the Storm Troopers. Selde told Hitler about this, and Hitler was very unhappy. Afterwards, Roehm asked Hitler to disband the Steel Helmet League, or to make the Steel Helmet League fully subject to the command of the National Socialist Party. His attitude was very tough. Hitler himself had already leaned to the right at this time, and he was deeply dissatisfied with the left-leaning members of the National Socialist Party. He also felt that Roehm had other ambitions, so he refused. This is one point of the conflict between the left and right wings. The second request was that Roehm allowed his subordinates to be added to the National Defense Army when the National Defense Army was expanded in the future. The British military reduction plan had allowed the German National Defense Army to expand to 200,000 to 300,000. Once this point is recognized internationally, the German National Defense Army will naturally be greatly expanded. If Roehm's plan is followed, the Storm Troopers can select members to supplement the National Army at that time. In this way, the honorary status and salary of the Storm Troopers can be increased. However, the National Defense Army strongly opposed this, because the social status and usual training of the National Defense Army are far from comparable to the Storm Troopers. Indiscriminate joining will not only hinder the discipline of the National Defense Army, but also reduce its status. Hitler was very difficult to deal with between the two forces. At the same time, because he was dissatisfied with the left-leaning of the Storm Troopers, he was willing to compromise with the opinions of the National Defense Army and cut back on the team he had created. The steps he took were to replace Roehm and to reduce the Storm Troopers. The two orders issued by Hitler in early June were the first steps in his predetermined plan. These two orders were: (1) Roehm was given a month's leave due to physical indisposition, and he was allowed to go to Dalmating to recuperate; (2) The Storm Troopers were given a month's vacation. During the vacation, they were not allowed to wear uniforms or hold meetings and parades. The intention of these two orders was very obvious in resolving Roehm's power. Therefore, Roehm had no choice but to obey the order and go to Dalmating to recuperate. However, it was not long before he sneaked back to Munich and secretly plotted something wrong. Therefore, Hitler, Goering, and others knew about it, and they resolved the conspiracy of Roehm and others with lightning speed.

Therefore, Hitler had already understood this coup, and the prevention and response were all predetermined. Hitler's right-leaning was also fully exposed by this incident. A Reuters dispatch from Paris on the 7th of this month said, "On August 1st, the Prime Minister met with General Fei Lizi, the Chief of Staff of the National Defense Army, General Bai Longbao, the Minister of National Defense, and General Li Qinuo of the Ministry, and explained to them that only he himself, as the head of state, could save the civil war. He also said that he was prepared to make a guarantee in writing, stating that after he took the position of Marshal of the Army, he would never use his position to discriminate against the National Defense Army, and he would be responsible for weakening the socialist tendencies of the National Socialist Party and adopting the suggestions of the National Defense Army on domestic and foreign policy matters." From this, we can know Hitler's attitude. Moreover, Hitler has recently reduced the Storm Troopers from 2.5 million to 800,000, which shows that Roehm's rebellion was by no means Roehm's fault alone.
