Educational News

Ministry of Education Inspector 175

Recent inspection of Hunan vocational education improvement suggestions (below)

(B) Regarding each school:

(1) Provincial Senior Agricultural Vocational School: In the past, due to the small area, students had difficulty with practical training, so it was difficult to be confident in their technical skills. Now that a new school site has been found, and the field is barely sufficient, a relocation and construction plan is underway. It seems that transformation is possible. In the future, special attention should be paid to the teaching of agriculture and forestry, and to the improvement and promotion of local production. Is the sericulture department suitable for local needs? In the few counties in southern and western Hunan where the sericulture industry has declined, is there any hope of reversing this? Is it possible for the quality and sales of silk cocoons to be on par with those of the provinces in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River? These questions are all necessary considerations for whether the school should continue to run the sericulture department. The school should decide on the conditions for setting up the department based on local conditions, and it is not necessary to stick to the original subjects, which are difficult to develop.

(2) Provincial Senior Industrial Vocational School: Both the mechanical and electrical engineering departments have a considerable foundation in practical training equipment. If the practical training is carried out properly, the mechanical engineering graduates can bear the manufacturing tasks of ordinary machine factories, and the electrical engineering graduates can also serve as managers of ordinary power plants. However, there are not many factories in the province, and students must develop outwards, so the employment situation is very difficult. All the equipment in the dyeing and weaving department is also sufficient for use. Although the applied chemistry department has experiments in papermaking, leather making, and soap making, the equipment is simple. The products of these two departments lack production value. They should be improved according to the following methods: A. According to the current vocational education situation in Hunan Province, the university's engineering college should be the center for training advanced technical personnel, and the senior industrial school should be the place for creating practical production personnel. Therefore, factory practice in senior industrial schools should not be broad and superficial, resulting in circular learning without any specialization. Attention should be paid to specialized skills in order to be practical. B. Mechanics can focus on imitation (see previous article) in order to promote it. For example, the various looms made by the school have excellent results and are not expensive. School factories can adopt them, which is a clear effect. The machinery that the chemistry department should add can be gradually manufactured by the school to make it complete. The design drawings of other ordinary industries (such as printing, flour milling, compression molding, iron making, slicing, dyeing, oil making, etc., which do not belong to the scope of precision and large-scale industries) should also be gradually collected widely as materials for students' research. C. If the practical training factory can be expanded, it can engage in an organization dedicated to production and manufacturing according to the factory system. For example, the clothing, leather goods, and cleaning and hygiene products used by students in various schools can be manufactured in large quantities, which can not only be used as a promotion of local production, but also as a model for students to operate production businesses. D. Select several kinds of practical training products and make them into marketable commodities. The design, style, decoration, and price should be researched and prepared. If you are confident, you can submit a request to the Education Department to raise temporary funds or guarantees to borrow money from the bank for turnover. At the same time, vocational supplementary classes can be attached to train apprentices.

(3) Private Xiuye Senior Agricultural Vocational School has been experimenting with improving rice seeds for many years, and has achieved results in increasing yields, which are being promoted. However, because this project is not very effective, it has now changed its approach and started with experimenting with rural side occupations, which is more profitable. The practical effect will be great in the future. The school is located outside Changsha City in an area with mountains and rivers. The field is barely sufficient. The vocational teachers lead students to work, which is quite serious. Students' practical training is divided into two types: divided land and public farming. Most of them wear short clothes and bare feet, cultivating in the fields, which can be regarded as hard work and training. However, judging from the school's funding and setting conditions, it should be appropriate to specialize in agricultural vocational subjects. The rural normal school department should find ways to gradually end it.

(4) The Private Gongshu Senior Civil Engineering Vocational School was founded by the carpentry trade union. The construction sites in the provincial capital and neighboring areas can all lead students to practice. Graduates also do not worry about finding employment, so they are very confident in the development of their careers. However, the rise and fall of construction engineering is related to the surplus and deficit of social economy. According to the trade union's statistics, the total value of construction engineering in Changsha City alone is more than 20 million yuan per year. In recent years, the trend has been upward. However, it is difficult to determine whether this constant state can be maintained. It is best to contact the trade unions in neighboring provinces to accept students from Wuhan, Yichang, Jiujiang, and Nanchang (based on those recommended by the trade unions) to broaden the training, which will be beneficial to both talent digestion and career improvement.

(5) The works of students in the normal and Western painting departments of the Private Huazhong Art School are still impressive. However, the equipment is simple and the scope is narrow. Charcoal drawing is the basic practice of Western methods. There are too few models, and it is difficult to accurately learn with the heart, hands, and eyes. Sketching goes without saying. If you strive for pleasing color matching in watercolor and oil painting, the foundation has not been established, and it will ultimately be empty and unrealistic. This point should be paid attention to. Chinese painting works are better than Western paintings, because people with higher talent can easily understand the artistic conception. However, obtaining its similarity is ultimately not as good as starting with meticulous brushwork of flowers, birds, and figures, and then learning freehand brushwork, which is more practical.

(6) Yueyang Private Hubin Middle School has gradually increased the settings for horticulture since it was changed to an agricultural department. The school has spacious school buildings, beautiful scenery, and is located in a fertile area on the side of Dongting Lake, which is most suitable for running an agricultural department. It is a pity that the funding is insufficient and the field cannot be expanded, so progress is difficult. If there are no security problems with the case of the Yueyang County Government entrusting the management of Junshan, it may be accepted. If the school's financial resources are insufficient, it can jointly convene leaders from all walks of life in the province and bank leaders with the county government to form a committee to handle it, because Junshan is a famous tea-producing area and a scenic spot. If managed properly, it will benefit the local area. (End)

It is heard that the Fengtian Printing Bureau is about to distribute the textbooks to bookshops for joint sales. From then on, the Three Principles of the People textbooks will disappear in the four northeastern provinces.

Ministry of Education Circular 177

Measures to Commemorate Confucius

(Nanjing, 25th) The Ministry of Education ordered all departments and bureaus and all public and private colleges and universities above the junior college level, saying that when holding a Confucius birthday commemoration, Confucius's portrait should be placed in front of Sun Yat-sen's portrait. The Confucius Commemoration Song is temporarily missing. The Ministry also ordered that item 3 of the Confucius Birthday Commemoration Measures, Confucius's brief history, (the sage was born in 1462 BC) is a mistake, and should be 2462 BC, (died in 1390 BC, which is also a mistake). The order is hereby given for compliance and correction, and subordinates are instructed to correct it as a whole.

This City's Elementary and Secondary Schools 179

Labor Pre-Exhibition to Open on Schedule

Education Bureau Orders Schools to Send Representatives to Attend the Opening Ceremony

Schools Closed for Half a Day During the Exhibition Period to Visit the Venue

Venue Divided into Two Locations: First Shangwen, Second Xicheng

The preliminary exhibition of labor course achievement works of elementary and secondary schools in this city is scheduled to be held for three days starting on the 29th of this month, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. The Municipal Education Bureau specially instructed the schools yesterday to send representatives to participate in the opening ceremony at 9:00 am on the 29th. Schools may be closed for half a day during the exhibition period to visit the venue. The details of each situation are recorded as follows:

Scheduled Opening The Labor Pre-Exhibition is scheduled to hold an opening ceremony at 9:00 am on the 29th of this month. The Municipal Education Bureau stipulates that the number of representatives that each school should send to participate in the opening ceremony is as follows: A. Each vocational school and normal school should send at least four teachers and staff representatives and twenty student representatives. B. Each elementary school in the Hunan District of Shanghai should send at least two teachers and staff representatives and six student representatives. C. Each elementary school in the Zhabei District should send at least two teachers and staff representatives and four student representatives. D. Each elementary school in the rural area should send at least one teacher and staff representative and two student representatives.

Half-Day Closure During the meeting and exhibition period, each school may be closed for half a day to visit the venue. The visiting dates for each school are stipulated as follows: (1) August 29, Normal schools and elementary schools in the Hunan District of Shanghai visit (2) August 30, Vocational schools and elementary schools in the Zhabei District visit (3) August 31, Middle schools and elementary schools in the rural area visit.

Additional Venue The exhibition venue was originally designated to be the Municipal Shangwen Elementary School. Now, due to the large number of exhibits from various schools, the Education Bureau has also designated the Municipal Xicheng Elementary School as the second venue. The achievements of middle schools are displayed in Shangwen Elementary School, and the achievements of elementary schools are displayed in Xicheng Elementary School. At that time, the exhibits from each school will be sent to the venue for separate handling.

Custody Measures From the day of display to the end of the exhibition, each school with exhibits must send its own staff to be responsible for arranging, keeping, and collecting the exhibits. During the exhibition period, the staff should explain the inquiries of visitors in detail. The staff who attend the meeting every day must also wear a badge with the school seal for identification.

Record of the Opening of the Annual Meeting of the Science Society of China 180

Famous domestic scholars all attended

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek sent Chen Bu Lei to deliver a speech

(Lushan Communication) The 19th annual meeting of the Science Society of China was held at the Lushan Lian Valley Youth Association on the 22nd of this month. The Chinese Geographical Society, the Chinese Botanical Society, and the Chinese Zoological Society also held their annual meetings here. A total of more than 140 members attended. Famous domestic scholars Ren Shuyong, Zhu Zhen, Bing Nongshan, Hu Xiansu, Wu Liande, Xue Dunfu, Liu Yimou, Wang Diancun, Qian Chongshu, Jiang Menglin, Chen Bulei, Chen Qinghua, Zhang Qi, etc., all attended the meeting. The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 am on the 22nd, presided over by Xiao Chunjin, chairman of the annual meeting, who delivered an opening speech. Then, Ren Shuyong, president of the Science Society of China, reported on the establishment process and general situation of the society, stating that the Science Society of China was established in the fourth year of the Republic of China. From the fourth to the eighth year of the Republic of China, it was the germination period. From the ninth to the fourteenth year, it was the transplantation period. From the fifteenth year to the present, it has been the development period, and listed the work of the Science Society, such as translation, publication of publications (Science Magazine and Science Pictorial, etc.), science lectures, etc. Then, Zhu Kezhen, president of the Chinese Geographical Society, Qian Yunong, president of the Chinese Botanical Society, and Bing Nongshan, the person in charge of the Chinese Zoological Society, successively reported on the mission and affairs of each society (the Zoological Society was established this year).

(Chiang Kai-shek's speech) After the report, Chen Bulei delivered a speech on behalf of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, stating that the Chairman attached great importance to the Science Society. Recently, due to his hard work presiding over the military officer training corps, he felt unwell and could not come to participate in person. He specially ordered himself to represent him. The content of the speech was to widely expound on "investigating things to acquire knowledge and utilizing life to promote prosperity", and to encourage the Science Society to engage in academic research and scientific application. Then, Chairman Xiong was invited to deliver a speech, stating that the gathering of celebrities and scholars of the Science Society in Lushan adds luster to the mountains and rivers. Science can give life and kill people, and it can prosper a country and destroy a country. It is extremely important for the revival of the country and nation. I hope that attention will be paid to the application of science to revitalize the country, and I hope that experts will provide guidance on the various facilities in this province.

(Chen and Wang's speeches) Then, Chen Lifu, a member of the Central Committee, was invited to give a speech, stating that scientific research should focus on organizing our country's inherent knowledge, and should not be completely erased with the three words "unscientific". We must strive to integrate it so that all knowledge can be scientific. He also advocated that scientific research should pay attention to popularization so that the public can be affected by it. Then, Wang Xueting, Minister of Education, was invited to give a speech, which was divided into two points: 1. Pay attention to scientific research and its application. 2. Pay attention to the improvement of research on scientific education. Finally, Cheng Shihuang, Director of the Department of Education, gave a speech, expounding the significance of the Science Society meeting from the perspective of Lushan's history and geography, stating that the ancestor of Lushan's development was Master Yuan of the Jin Dynasty, who founded the Lotus Society as a Buddhist group. During the Song Dynasty, Mr. Zhu and Mr. Lu lectured at the Ludong Academy, which was the source of scholars from all directions. Today, there is the Science Society, which is opening a new era for Chinese academic culture after Buddhism and Neo-Confucianism.

(Society Meeting) After the speeches, a group photo was taken and the meeting was adjourned. In the afternoon at 2:00, the society meeting was held. At 4:00, papers were read. There were society meetings and reading of papers every morning, and in the afternoon there were mostly tours of scenic spots and banquets. The provincial government banquet was scheduled for 6:00 pm on the 23rd. The Economic Committee, the Jiujiang Municipal Committee, the Lushan Management Bureau, and the New Life Promotion General Association jointly hosted the event on the afternoon of the 24th. The annual meeting was scheduled for six days and will be closed on the 27th. After the closing, some members will go down the mountain and transfer to Nanchang to hold public scientific lectures. It is heard that Director Cheng will rush back to Nanchang on the 25th to take care of everything.

Department Orders to Reduce 181

Wuxi Elementary School Education Fees

Zang, Director of the Wuxi Education Bureau, submitted a request to the provincial government regarding the reduction of county education fees by the Department of Education, requesting that the recurrent expenses be maintained and issued as before. It is learned that Director Zang returned to Wuxi from the province at 4:00 pm yesterday. It is reported that regarding the issue of reducing education fees, the Department took into account the inevitable autumn famine and made an overall calculation. As to whether the county can maintain its old education budget, it will be determined after the Department sends personnel to Wuxi for calculation. It is also heard that Commissioner Deng, sent by the Department, has left the province to work in neighboring counties and will arrive in Wuxi soon. According to general predictions, the county's education funds and temporary activity fees will inevitably be cut. Even the recurrent expenses will probably be discounted. However, in order to take care of the future of elementary education, Director Zang is determined to do everything possible to exceed the 60% amount set by the Department, so that the advancement of elementary education will not be greatly affected.

Mongolian Tibetan Academy Preparatory Meeting 185

Pan Gongzhan Reports on Enrollment

Regular Meetings of School Trustees to be Convened

The Mongolian Tibetan Academy held a preparatory committee meeting at the Lianhuan Society at 3:00 pm yesterday. Pan Gongzhan, Yu Zuoting, Shi Wenran, Jin Houcheng, Liu Baihe, Chen Zhaorui, Qian Shoutie, He Ziyan, Wang Yansong, Luosang Qingpi, Cheng Linsheng, Ma Gongyu, etc. attended the meeting, which was chaired by Pan Gongzhan.

Chairman's Report Chairman Pan reported on the enrollment situation. The new student entrance examination was held at the Xueyi Society on the 15th and 16th of this month. The subjects were Party Principles, Chinese, History, Geography, and Mathematics. There were 108 applicants for the training class and 3 applicants for the advanced class. An examination committee was held at the Lianhuan Society on the 21st to discuss the admission of new students. The results were published in the Morning Post on the 23rd. There were 40 admitted students and 20 alternate students in the training class. Students have been notified separately. As for the advanced class, due to the small number of students, whether to open the class or not will be determined after each monastery recommends students to the academy. Among the 40 admitted students in the training class, 8 have graduated from universities and independent colleges, 4 have studied at universities and independent colleges, 1 has graduated from a vocational school, 25 have graduated from high school, and 2 have graduated from the old-style normal school.

Resolutions (1) Proposed to convene a meeting of the board of directors of this academy. It was resolved that most of the school directors of this academy are out on business and it is difficult to gather them all at once. It is proposed to convene them again when the Fifth National Congress in the capital is completed and the directors arrive in Shanghai. (2) The Mongolian and Tibetan Teachers Training Class should have a director in charge of handling all matters. It was resolved to recommend Qian Shoutie, the director of affairs of this academy, to serve concurrently on a temporary basis. (3) Students in the Mongolian and Tibetan Teachers Training Class will not be charged any fees except for a deposit. (4) The curriculum of the Teachers Training Class was determined to be drafted by the Academic Affairs Office. (5) The various equipment for this academy was resolved to be handled by the Office of General Affairs. (6) Whether to continue recruiting students for the Tibetan Language Advanced Class and open the academy was resolved to notify alternate students that those who wish to enter may study in the class. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

Provincial Yu Tang People's Education Center 186

Holding Training Classes for People's Education Personnel

The Yu Tang People's Education Center was founded by Niu Tiesheng and was changed to a provincial institution last year. The center, recognizing a shortage of rural people's education personnel, has specially obtained approval from the Department of Education to establish training classes for people's education service personnel starting from September of this year. These classes will focus on rural improvement and serve as the central hub for cultivating rural construction personnel. The classes will emphasize a "learning by doing" approach, using the surrounding Wu Fang Li area as an experimental zone. Enrollment is scheduled to begin on September 1st, with a requirement of junior high school graduation or equivalent education level. The quota is thirty students, limited to the guidance area of the center, including students from Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, Jinshan, Fengxian, Chuansha, Baoshan, Jiading, Qingpu, etc. Tuition, board, and lodging are all free. Detailed regulations and procedures have been distributed to the education bureaus of each county and can also be obtained directly from the center.

Sino-French National 187

Engineering School Graduates Go to Belgium

Hua Yi'gan and Zhou Jia'mo Set Sail Yesterday

The Sino-French National Institute of Engineering has been jointly operated by the Chinese and French governments for more than a decade. This school is an industrial vocational school that has always adhered to strict principles, cultivating talent. Each year, outstanding students are selected and sent to France, Belgium, and other countries for further study. To date, more than thirty graduates have completed their studies and returned to China. This time, eight undergraduate students graduated, with Hua Yi'gan and Zhou Jia'mo ranking at the top. The school then requested the Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Committee to fund their studies in Belgium, and they set sail yesterday. The remaining students have also been introduced to various locations for employment.

Da Gong Vocational School 188

Expands Free Enrollment Quota

The Da Gong Vocational School and its affiliated junior high school, located in the Nanshi district of this city, were originally scheduled to open on the 28th of this month. However, due to the unfinished renovation of the new school building, the opening has been postponed to September 6th, with fee payment scheduled for the 6th and 7th, and registration on the 8th and 9th. Classes will temporarily be held at the old school building on Qiao Jia Road, outside the Xiao Nan Men, starting on the 10th. It is expected that the school will move to its new location on Longhua Road, near Ju Men Road, on October 1st. It is reported that the school has already received three times more new students than old students this year, and requests for admission are still pouring in. Therefore, an additional entrance examination will be held on September 5th to avoid disappointment. The school's principal, Mr. Lin Meiyan, recognizing the impact of rural bankruptcy on students' ability to pursue education due to economic hardship, has donated his salary to increase the number of free enrollment places. Both new and old students can apply for assistance, and the number of scholarship places will also be expanded, with service student positions added. This dual approach of rewards and subsidies is a great opportunity for those who cannot afford tuition in the midst of the current economic downturn.

Sports News

Shanghai International Tennis Semifinals, Day One 191

United States and China Dominate

Japan and England Completely Defeated in Singles Yesterday

Exciting Doubles Matches Expected Today Between China and England

In Addition to Two Doubles Matches, There Will Also Be Two Singles Matches Between China and England

The Rotary Cup Shanghai International Tennis Tournament, with China vs. England and the United States vs. Japan, held its semifinals simultaneously at the Shanghai Tennis Club yesterday afternoon. Despite the scorching sun, there were still over three hundred spectators. In the four singles matches, the United States and China both achieved complete victories. The performances of the American players Carlsen and Squire were exceptionally beautiful, surpassing their previous performances, forcing the Japanese players Machida and Sudo to concede defeat. China's Zheng Zhaojia and Wang Wenzheng played casually and were assured of victory. England's Stock and Forbes were unable to fight and collapsed at the mere sight of their opponents. This afternoon will be the doubles matches for the four countries, but because the English side cannot spare the time on Monday, the final two singles matches will be held simultaneously today. Therefore, the qualification for the finals between China and England will be decided this afternoon. The details of yesterday's battles are recorded below:

United States Wins Against Japan 192

Carlsen Overpowers Machida: The match between the American first singles player Carlsen and the Japanese player Machida began at 3:00 PM. Both players performed well, with long rallies and net interceptions that were quite impressive. Carlsen's technique, in particular, has improved significantly, as evidenced by his straight-set victory over Wang Wenzheng the other day, which was no accident. Machida's long rallies from deep behind the baseline often caused Carlsen to struggle to keep up. However, Carlsen made good use of his net play, which proved to be very effective, greatly troubling Machida, who lost two sets with scores of 6-4 and 6-3. In the third set, Machida had a very good chance of winning, leading 5-3 and then 5-4. Machida was serving with a score of 3-2, just needing one more point to win the set. Unexpectedly, he hit a ball out of bounds, making the score 40-40 (3-3). He then lost the game, making the set score 5-5. Carlsen then took the lead at 6-5. Machida tied it again, but Carlsen finally won two consecutive games, resulting in a straight-set victory.

6-4

Carlsen (USA) {6-3} Machida (Japan)

8-6

Squire Defeats Sudo: The American second singles player Squire's skills are also far from what they used to be. He made good use of chop shots, reaching deep behind the baseline, and sweeping to both corners. He had very few net touches and out-of-bounds balls, and he was good at running, with a very good grasp of saving the ball. He fought by moving back and forth, dashing all over the court. Japan's Sudo, although also a steady and enduring player, ultimately failed due to slightly inferior skills. Squire won the first two sets easily with scores of 6-3 and 6-1. In the third set, Sudo led 3-1 and 5-3. Squire captured the serve game, making the score 5-4. Sudo was serving, but Squire lost four consecutive points, so Sudo won the set 6-4. In the fourth set, Squire returned to his original form and won it easily with a score of 6-2.

6-3

Squire (USA) {6-1} Sudo (Japan)

4-6

6-2

China Wins Against England 193

Zheng Zhaojia Wins Against Stock: The China-England match followed the US-Japan match. This year, China did not use the veteran players Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai for singles, but instead used the rising stars Zheng Zhaojia and Wang Wenzheng. Regardless of whether they win the championship, this approach is very appropriate and can raise the profile of the tennis community, letting people know that in addition to Lin and Qiu, there are also players like Zheng and Wang who deserve attention. Zheng's opponent was Stock, and it was a one-sided situation. Zheng took the first four games without any effort, but then he made careless mistakes, often sending the ball into the net or out of bounds, allowing his opponent to catch up to 5-4. He only won 6-4. In the second set, the opponent was too sluggish, and Zheng did not show much excitement, just casually responding, and won 6-1. In the third set, Zheng won again 6-3. Zheng's strategy was quite clever, and his ball control was also very skilled, but he still made too many double faults on serves, which should be paid attention to.

6-4

Zheng Zhaojia (China) {6-1} Stock (England)

6-3

Wang Wenzheng Defeats Forbes: England's Forbes was a finalist in last year's Shanghai Junior Singles, with more than enough stability, but not enough attack. Wang Wenzheng was just testing the waters, and a straight-set victory was expected. However, Wang's shots were very polite, just casually responding, winning 6-3, 6-2, in a leisurely manner. In the third set, Wang led 4-1, and Forbes caught up to 5-4, but Wang won 6-4 in the end. Wang's skills have not improved, and his ball control has no variation. If he encounters someone of equal strength, he will definitely suffer. He really should use more intelligence to explore.

6-3

Wang Wenzheng (China) {6-2} Forbes (England)

6-4

Comparable to the White Rainbow Team, Both on Land and Water

Diligent Sports Monthly 199

Swimming and Tennis Special Issue Published

Women's Realm

Who is Promoting Cosmetics? 203

— Yun Shang

In the newspapers of the past month, the alarming figures of foreign cosmetic imports have been repeatedly published. But upon closer inspection, this year's first half, including lace, is only worth 1.5 million. If we actually knew the economic and political status of women in Shanghai, there would be nothing to be surprised about.

According to a recent report, Shanghai has a total of 3.4 million residents, half of whom are women, totaling 1.7 million. Excluding those who push dung carts, sell vegetables, and live in straw shacks in Caojiadu, Yangshupu, Pudong, and other areas of poor farmers and workers, women from ten to fifty years old, without exception, automatically purchase cosmetics. And those dancers, stars, socialites, concubines, and various types of prostitutes buy even more than ordinary people each month. Assuming that women who buy cosmetics account for slightly less than one-third of all women in Shanghai each month—500,000 people—then the average amount of foreign cosmetics purchased per person is only 50 cents.

But when we look at the cost of cosmetics used by those dancers and social stars, it's more than 50 cents a day. Because 50 cents a day is only 15 yuan a month, which is far from the truth. According to my estimate, there are 200,000 women in Shanghai who use more than one yuan worth of cosmetics each month, including hair tonic, eyebrow pencils, rouge, lip balm, powder, nail polish, perfume, soap, cold cream, various beauty products, and so on. If this is true, then there are about 6 million cosmetic costs on these women each month, not including the miscellaneous expenses such as hair perms, utensils, and maid wages.

Don't men use cosmetics? Hair tonic is now used more by men than women in the city. Many men also use cold cream and perfume. Let's ignore that for now.

What we should be studying now is the motivation and need of the 500,000 Shanghai women who buy an average of 50 cents worth of foreign cosmetics each month. Among them, the ones who need cosmetics the most are those women who live a "prostitute-like life." The number of these women in Shanghai is alarming, ranging from the concubines of high officials and wealthy people to the "wild chickens" who solicit customers on the street, including school queens, office flowers, female shop assistants who serve as signage in shops, and social stars who specialize in accompanying people to dance. This type of woman uses the most cosmetics. However, the reason why they must use a large amount of cosmetics is entirely to maintain their "business." A sweaty dancer or prostitute who does not attract male customers—players—is undoubtedly an absolute fact. Even the title of "Queen" in those schools cannot be obtained by a female student who does not wear makeup, does not perm her hair, does not use perfume and nail polish, and wears cloth clothes and shoes. Moreover, it is a confirmed fact that part of the cosmetics used by this type of woman is often given by men.

In this way, the truth of the matter is clear. The use of large quantities of cosmetics on special women is equivalent to the coal and water needed for a locomotive to run, or the gasoline used by a car. Although the running of trains and cars is increasingly old and damaged, the consumption of coal, water and gasoline only bears a relationship to its own power to be used. How is the case of a prostitute-style woman and cosmetics different?

In Shanghai, apart from the working masses, there are frustrated politicians and bureaucrats, wealthy idlers, and young playboys. With this group of treasures concentrated in Shanghai, countless prostitute-style women live wasteful lives day and night, wrapped in cosmetics, eating, drinking, and having fun.

Then who exactly buys cosmetics and needs cosmetics? Is the large import of foreign cosmetics the fault of the dancers and prostitutes themselves who use a lot of cosmetics? Can we still bear to blame them?

In short, is it not a travesty that the country is so disorganized that its domestic market is not occupied by its own industry and has no way to resist the economic invasion of foreign races, and is the blame for the import of cosmetics placed on the pitiful prostitutes?

August 15th, at the Women's Resonance Society

Soviet Wives 204

— Written by Anra Louse Strong, Translated by Liang Qiu

(This is a self-account by an American woman who married a Soviet man. From this, one can observe the various perspectives of Soviet women on relationships. The Soviet Union is a mysterious country in the eyes of the world, and these perspectives are worth our attention. Therefore, I specially translated it for the readers.)

Recently, while traveling and giving speeches in the United States, I happened to have dinner at an old friend's house. After the meal, I mentioned that I had gotten married in Moscow two years ago. Suddenly, everyone at the table looked at me as if surprised, and in their questions, they expressed their doubts and misunderstandings about our marriage.

Elsewhere, a girlfriend interrogated me about the so-called "personal life" of Soviet people for hours. Although I answered her faithfully, I knew she still couldn't understand. Later, while discussing some admirable human virtues, I said that my husband possessed this virtue to a high degree. "I think you 'like' your husband," she said in surprise. This time, I was really annoyed. "Why would I live with someone I don't like?" I replied. But from her conversation, I wondered why she lived with her husband. Because she frankly told me that she despised certain characteristics of her husband - his almost useless honesty, which made him a pleasant companion but was not conducive to making money under capitalism. Having dinner at her house, this unvarnished and harsh conversation - from her dissatisfaction with a useless husband to her wandering, wasteful children - was very unpleasant to listen to. What traditional forces, what economic oppression, made her endure such unpleasant dinners day after day?

If such disgusting conversations occurred during meals in a Soviet family, their simple separation would be the end of it. Life is so short, so precious, that it is not worth wasting on unpleasant companions. Sometimes, in their professions, people must endure unpleasant companions in order to receive training and achieve career success. But the purpose of family is not for training and career; it is only for recreation and rest in life. Why should humans endure such unpleasant companions?

I know that stating the purpose of family in this way seems very reasonable to Soviet wives, but it challenges two kinds of ancient marriage concepts: one is the family concept advocated by the church, and the other is the family concept under feudal capitalism. Such as Bacon's view of family, the concept of children that makes many mothers endure lifelong pain, the concept of relying on others, etc. - these concepts disappear like smoke in Soviet marriages.

In the eyes of Soviet wives, marriage is not related to religion, law, or property rights. These things are completely unimportant to our lives. No one has a lot of money, so property rights are very simple. What was owned before marriage remains individually owned after marriage; what is acquired after marriage is jointly owned by both. The wages earned by the couple are jointly owned and used, with a very small portion saved for the future. Religion still exists among those who need it; church weddings still happen sometimes. The law also exists; most, though not all, marriages are properly registered, but no one would ask their friends if their marriage is registered.

For us, the essence of marriage is lasting friendship, making physiological, mental, and emotional life satisfying and fulfilling. How long it will last, only future facts can tell; we hope it will last a lifetime, but we cannot guarantee it. For those who marry, almost everyone, marriage means mutually participating in future life through raising children. No normal person does not want to have children. I can't recall a single old maid among my Soviet acquaintances. But marriage is just a kind of friendship; and children are the only key to future life. Personal "love" is just a song in an opera to us; its complex and noisy chords only occupy a very limited time in the entire play.

If our marriage is so informal, without restrictions or coercion, simply registered at the government office, sometimes not even registered, and seems not to be a "proper marriage" in the eyes of people outside the Soviet Union, then we must also say that marriages in capitalist society, as we see in novels and newspapers, are either terrifying or ridiculous. Announcing marriage in newspapers seems very strange to us. If, like in America, our marriage news were filled with social news and our photos appeared among many white flowers, boasting and exaggerating our personal feelings like that, we would feel very ashamed. We announce our marriage to a few close friends, often after the wedding rather than before.

We are also not hypocritical in not wanting to announce. If we receive scientific honors, or become a leading driver in a collective farm, or win a manufacturing award in a factory, we would feel proud to have our names published in the newspaper. If our photo could be raised high on a pole during the May Day celebration and our comrades reported to the world that we are warriors, that would make us feel supremely honored. Because these are our public actions, worthy of praise or criticism. Marriage is our private life, a personal matter!

The Ideal Woman in the Eyes of Japanese Female Students 205

— Du Bu

— Healthy and dignified —

— Virtuous Mother, Good Wife —

In Japan, the phrase "extraordinary times" can be seen and heard everywhere now. The government is a government of extraordinary times, national policies are policies of extraordinary times, and even when friends meet, they say, "These are extraordinary times." What are "extraordinary times"? People don't seem to understand very clearly. But we know that the so-called "extraordinary times" means that Japanese imperialism is using all its power to annex China and seize hegemony in the Pacific. To achieve this goal, they vaguely use the phrase "extraordinary times" to lure the Japanese people, advocating absolute patriotism, aggression, hero worship, martial spirit, and widespread creation of a war mentality within the country, so that the Japanese people immersed in this poison enthusiastically support Japan's aggression against China, hatred of the Soviet Union, and its hegemonic policy against the United States. Therefore, a "war atmosphere" envelops the entire Japan.

In this era, what are general Japanese women like? What kind of ideals do they have under this "extraordinary times" atmosphere? This is a question worth paying attention to. Recently, the Japanese Ministry of Education, perhaps to test the extent to which the poison they have cultivated has permeated the Japanese people, especially women, conducted a survey among women in Tokyo and other regions, asking them to answer the question "What are the elements of a modern ideal woman?" According to their published statistics, the elements of an ideal woman that Japanese women hope for are as follows:

A. Statistical results from 1,360 senior female students from fourteen schools in Tokyo:

(1) Health. (2) Femininity. (3) Cheerfulness. (4) Profound interests. (5) Strong will. (6) Sense of chastity. (7) Domesticity. (8) Understanding of social situations. (9) Common sense.

B. Statistical results from 3,261 senior female students from thirty-one schools in other regions:

(1) Health. (2) Cheerfulness. (3) Economic awareness. (4) Femininity. (5) Dignified appearance. (6) Sense of chastity. (7) Common sense. (8) Cultured. (9) Profound interests. (10) Strong will.

Among these, health is the most frequently mentioned element in both Tokyo and other regions. 69% in Tokyo and 64% in other regions, more than half, believe it is an element of a modern ideal woman.

From these statistics, it is clear that women still exhibit feminine characteristics. First, we do not see any of the frenzy or brutality of "extraordinary times" here. They are still very peaceful and seem unaffected by the "extraordinary times." The "war atmosphere" and hero worship are still absent. They honestly seek health, and health first seems to be the ideal element that Japanese women imagine. Second, the education of Japanese virtuous mother and good wife ideology is still deeply rooted. Women are domestic, feminine, and have a sense of chastity. In short, they are people of the family, not like men who participate in social activities. The life of creating new history, the life of shaking the world, the new life of liberated women, does not seem to have formed a concept in their minds. Third, their hope is still to be a good housewife, a so-called good wife who serves her husband, a so-called virtuous mother, a docile weakling, a gentle follower. Therefore, they still cannot escape the scope of sacrifice in "extraordinary times" because they do not consider the pursuit of new ideals as the epitome of an ideal woman. However, this is only the view of a portion of female students. In addition, there are certainly many active women.

Career Paths for American Female Graduates 206

— Geng Longgen

Most American female students are very fond of playing. They have never had any understanding of the world. What they like is to dance and play with their favorite men every day, living a life without rules. But after they graduate, due to economic needs, they have to find a job. Some can get a job because their fathers or relatives and friends are important officials in companies, banks, or government agencies; others do not have this opportunity, but they can still go to the placement bureau at school to ask for their help. Below are some of the jobs that the placement bureau of a women's college in the eastern United States has listed as available for introduction:

1. Direct social work. 2. Assistant work in laboratories of hospitals, universities, factories, government agencies, etc. 3. Statistical work in banks, insurance companies, government agencies, etc. 4. Assistant editor work in newspapers and bookstores. 5. Clerk work in commercial and educational institutions. 6. Various jobs in large department stores. 7. Secretarial work that requires or does not require shorthand and typing. The jobs listed above are certainly not what graduates of women's colleges want to do, but there is no other way. However, there are still things they cannot do in these jobs. Therefore, the smart school authorities set up a cram school that can be completed in a few weeks during the vacation after graduation; in this way, on the one hand, they teach skills such as typing, shorthand, and statistics; on the other hand, for the limited positions in the placement bureau, they restrict them to students with better grades, and there is a fair distribution.

But what about those graduates who cannot be introduced by the placement office? Unless they get lucky, they can only go outside to solicit business for wireless companies, insurance companies, cosmetics factories, automobile companies, etc. They must pay the company a guarantee in advance; when they solicit business, they can get a little commission. If they cannot solicit business, not only can they not get a commission, but the company may even dismiss them.

Some become nannies for rich people's children or announcers for radio stations, etc. Still others have it really tough - they actually work as Dearies in department stores. A Dearie is a woman who has not been educated because she is beautiful and has a flirtatious attitude. She uses the word Dearie (darling) to address everyone. The owner of the department store hires them to attract vulgar customers.

Of course, being a teacher is a better job for women, but previous graduates have already occupied most of the positions, and newly graduated students inevitably lack the experience of those who have taught, so newly graduated students are rarely hired to teach. Therefore, parents of American female students now mostly advise their daughters to study medicine, pharmacy, law, commerce, and library management, etc., because these can make it easier for their daughters to find a way out after graduation.

A Living Person Arrives 207

— Bing Yun

When she received the news of her only younger sister's death, her heart was almost shattered. She seemed to be electrocuted, holding the letter in both hands, her face very pale, standing like a wooden chicken in front of the south-facing window. The letter slowly fell from her hand. Her knees softened, and she knelt down involuntarily. Her left hand was pressing on her throbbing heart, raising her right hand, just like a pastor praying in a church. The mother rolled on the ground like a madwoman; the neighbors all ran into their room. A bird's nest-like house was crowded with people, each saying a word to comfort her, but their shallow comfort only increased her sorrow. She cried more and more sadly, more and more fiercely, constantly beating her chest and stamping her feet. She thought of the tragic fate of her family, her wandering life, and felt as if ten thousand arrows were piercing her heart, her liver and intestines were broken!

She recalled the cruel past hatred that had left her body and mind crippled, and she limped back to her mother's house. Although it was a deep mother-daughter relationship, her mother, who was financially weak, actually wanted to refuse the return of her sick daughter with tears. Fortunately, her young sister, chivalrous and brave, stood up to shoulder the burden of her weak sister's life. She said: Mom! It will be tough for these two years! I will have a way when I graduate from high school. She went to school during the day and copied for people at night until late, counting the days one by one, and the expected time came closer and closer, but unexpectedly…

The old mother was already over sixty, and she didn't know who to entrust her remaining years to; and she herself was already married at home, and abandoned outside, so what could she rely on? Moreover, with this ugly disease, even benevolent gentlemen should avoid her.

She thought that heaven and earth created people, and she didn't know whether to call it "living" or to call it "dying"? How could she end up in this half-dead state? Her good sister, who was seventeen or eighteen years old, wanted to take on the livelihood of a family of three. However, her sister was so diligent on weekdays, but now she had failed the graduation exam, cutting off her life, cutting off the life of the whole family that she bore, so suffering drove her to her death!

Death! Why doesn't death leave enough dead people, but only wants to call the useful living to go? Her sister was very useful, even though she failed the exam. If she had died earlier, her sister might have had a lighter burden and would not have been so urgent to commit suicide, as if there was a thorn in her back. She thought that she, this living corpse, had implicated good people!

She thought confusedly for a long time, and in the dark room, there was no one but her mother's low breathing. She silently raised a glass of medicine to her lips, murmuring:

"A coffin pays for the body, everything is over;

Life arrives here, what does heaven care?"

Let's Talk About the "Virtuous Mother, Good Wife" System 208

— Yun Qi

Under the call of "Women! Return to the home!", the virtuous mother, good wife system has once again been praised by the general public. Regarding "virtuous mother, good wife," opinions on its interpretation have been very inconsistent throughout history. Generally, what people mean by a virtuous mother is one who absolutely obeys her husband's will, bears all the trivial matters of the family, works hard and complains little, and never resigns until death. A good wife is one who is solely responsible for the reproduction and education of her children. Such a virtuous mother and good wife, from the perspective of the historical development of class, that is, from the perspective of medieval feudal society, certainly has its own role or significance. However, in reality, this system has always been a one-sided obligation or morality, a cunning means used by men to bind women and make them become domestic slaves. Just like "chastity," it is only used by men to implement the restriction of women as their one-sided sexual tools. All one-sided obligations or morals are tools to oppress people and shackles to bind people.

Since the development of capitalism in various countries, countless rural and urban women have been forced to leave their families and enter factories and various social institutions (shops, schools! etc.). Thus, the medieval family system was destroyed, and women also gained more or less partial economic independence, no longer able to endure one-sided restrictions and oppression from men. Thus, the women's movement demanding women's liberation arose. And the initial goal of the women's movement was to break the old-fashioned family system and liberate the masses of women from domestic slavery. It opposes all the one-sided obligations, morals, and etiquette of the medieval family, and demands equal rights with men in the economic, political, and cultural aspects. From this, we can fully understand that anyone who advocates restoring the virtuous mother, good wife system is actually advocating restoring the family system of the medieval feudal era and all the tools that come with it to oppress women. In other words, it is to return to men all the achievements (such as the right to freedom of marriage, the right to inheritance, the right to vote...) that women have already gained through long-term struggle, and force them to return to the home to be domestic slaves and sexual tools again.

However, in reality, can the virtuous mother, good wife system be restored? For example, just from the perspective of China, hundreds of thousands of farmers have gone bankrupt, and the farmers' families have been destroyed from the root. Either the husband goes out to work, becomes a soldier (or even a bandit), or the wife goes out to work as a female worker or a nanny. In this situation, the whole family is scattered, so how can one talk about virtuous mothers and good wives? Pure worker families are even more miserable under the cruel exploitation and oppression of capitalists and the long-term threat of continuous unemployment. Talking about virtuous mothers and good wives to them is just a dream! In fact, the "virtuous mother, good wife" system that people are now advocating can only have some influence in the petty bourgeois class at most.

Although the virtuous mother, good wife system violates objective facts and cannot have much influence, we cannot but criticize this retrogressive movement and cannot but protest against it. We should tell those who are reversing the wheels of history: it is impossible to go against history, history must always move forward, and those who go against history will inevitably be crushed by the wheels of history. Modern women will never be subjected to such a foolish policy again.

(Creative Writing)

Children Companions 209

— Zi Gang

With a heart as heavy as a camel's burden, I walked on the sidewalk of the asphalt road. The streets of the big city are so noisy even during the day, only with fewer lights. Under the lights, everything is beautified. Even the sins of the devil are not as hideous as in the daytime.

Walking into XX Fang, I crossed a small path covered with coal ash, across from the watermelon peels and garbage piles, to pick up my repaired fountain pen.

"Is that...Xiao Yu!"

A hoarse throat called out to me. My heart jumped. I had been in Shanghai for almost half a month, and it was as if I had arrived in the desert, unable to even catch a glimpse of a single acquaintance from afar.

As soon as I looked up, a pair of familiar gray-yellow eyes! Followed by a string of female workers carrying boxes and small baskets behind the girl who had lost her youthful fire. Looking at the girl in front of me again, she was also wearing a tin can.

"A Qiu!" My eyes were probably wet. Happiness choked me. Looking at A Qiu, at least she had been redrawn, a circle smaller than five years ago. Thinner.

She held my shoulder:

"Xiao Yu, how are you? What brings you to Shanghai too?" Only those gray-yellow eyes hadn't changed. They might be less bright normally, but in these few minutes, they were excited.

"Something came up, I have to go home right away." I lied. Why disappoint someone? She had advised me to leave school like an older sister. Life had taught her to be more successful than anything else. She struggled in hardship, floating north and south like duckweed. I could only feel ashamed and lower my head. I couldn't forget her words when she let go of my hand in the north:

"Do you still want to hide away and read dead books? Do you still want to paste a paper gold coat on your flesh? You should drop your books early and throw yourself into real life." I remembered clearly that she even pinched my arm hard.

"Really, you forgot me, I forgot you!"

"Did you graduate? Are you putting on another set of clothes!"

This harsh mouth would never change! I nodded with a smiling face:

"Don't mention it, your story is more interesting than mine." Her environment only allowed her to study until elementary school. She wasn't discouraged. She followed her brothers' path and finally came to Shanghai with an old villager. She only sent a short note after going:

"Real life is more precious than diamonds. Here, people are aware of the meaning of working for the group. I labor, I temper in the burning furnace, I melt in the fluid, the fluid is mixed with me, this ball of fire wants to purify the universe."

It was simply an incomprehensible note. I wondered strangely why A Qiu had this perseverance. Perhaps it was a gift from the struggle with hardship!

"Are you driving a car?" I saw that this was the XX Yarn Factory.

She nodded: "Besides the blood and sweat that must flow for a grain of rice, here there is happiness that makes you feel the tension of life. The suffering is great enough, but, oh--no one is prepared to be a lifelong slave! We are tightly connected like new elastic bands!" Her hoarse voice became calm and slight, but it stuck to my heart like cement.

She accompanied me to get the pen and we parted at the factory gate. I was ridiculed a lot, but the ridicule only made me feel sincere.

"Coward!" I cursed myself on the way home. My heart was on fire.

Mr. Shi Zhen:

The Women's Garden is originally set up for women to express their opinions. In the past, seven or eight out of ten contributors were female students. If you have good works to contribute, you are welcome. - Editor

Commercial News

Finance 210

Previous Dynasty Overcompensated in Covering Shorts

Gold Speculators Rejoice as Sellers Gain Momentum

Although American Bank Exchange Rate Narrows

Still Drops Three Yuan and Three Jiao

The gold market, due to the previous dynasty's overcompensation in covering shorts, saw a decrease of 10,000 taels in market inventory. General sentiment predicted little hope for a resurgence of short-covering, so sellers boldly stepped forward. Speculator Wu also divested holdings, causing gold prices to shift from rising to falling. Although there was some struggle mid-course, buying interest was extremely weak, with supply exceeding demand, resulting in a decline. The laxity and oversupply of the exchange market likely fueled selling pressure. Initially, the exchange rate moved downwards uniformly in the morning due to flat conditions in the overseas silver market and a narrowing of the US exchange rate. American cotton rose eleven points, American wheat rose 0.0625, and stocks also rose 1.43 yuan. Public sentiment was greatly stirred by the sudden reduction of 0.125 in the American Bank exchange rate after the US government's intervention. The gross price of goods opened higher, rising to 63 yuan. In anticipation of trading, gold prices even rose as high as 4.8 jiao. Eventually, as the exchange market opened uneventfully, the high supply of resources caused a setback. Although there was some rebound after opening, the banks' appetite declined, and arbitrageurs aggressively divested. Although shorts covered, the market inventory had already decreased by approximately 10,000 taels, leading others to predict a lack of significant strength. In addition, the prior knowledge that the HSBC exchange rate was flat for the British pound but only narrowed by 0.125 for the US dollar caused slight disappointment, so prices retreated within the 60-yuan range. However, buyers were still unwilling to easily show weakness and were able to struggle within the 60-yuan range. Ultimately, due to weakening public sentiment and a lack of buying interest from Chinese merchants in the domestic market, prices declined. Reuters reported that the American firm Laiche Ferry & Co. announced today that it would increase its gold exports to $5,000,000, and Manhattan Bank also stated that it would increase its gold exports to $1,500,000. There was still a rebound after the decline, but the overall trend was difficult to sustain. Seeing the difficulty in turning the tide, buyers became weak, and unfavorable rumors circulated, further intensifying selling pressure in the market. The banks' domestic prices remained firm, and the situation was most fatigued at noon. Half-day trading was still active, but with continued exports of silver, the situation remained one of supply exceeding demand. October futures inventory had decreased to just over 31,000 taels after the aggressive short-covering the previous day. The half-day market situation is recorded below.

The morning opening price was 962.7 yuan, an increase of 4.6 yuan from the previous close. The opening price for goods was 2.8 jiao. The exchange market morning opening prices for near-term sales were 1 shilling, 4 pence, 0.05625 and 0.0625 for the British pound and 35 yuan for the US dollar. Zhaofeng Chang, Yongli Yuanmao, and Yongjin reached 4 yuan. Maijia Li and Citibank sold November US dollars at 0.1875, and Dafa Yongheng Yu Yifeng and Yongyicheng sold futures, retreating to around 2 yuan. Call Loan Rate Tight, Then Suddenly Eases 212

- Spot Silver Exports Slightly Moderate -

The market atmosphere in recent days has shown no signs of improvement for various commercial trends. The sudden rise in the call loan rate among foreign banks was attributed to excessive exports of spot silver, creating a shortage of spot funds in the market and causing public anxiety. Exports have indeed been significant. The government's recent increase in export tax rates has made exports unprofitable, leading to widespread inaction. As a result, the situation has eased, public sentiment has stabilized, and the call loan rate in the market has declined. Yesterday morning, both the morning and noon markets opened at 0.1 yuan, a sudden drop of 0.05 yuan from the previous day. The call loan rate plus water money was surprisingly loose, at 0.02-0.03 yuan, even free. The waterfront had ample funds, especially for call loans. Grain 221

Futures Flour Initially Rose, Then Became Flat

Yesterday in the flour market, after the morning opening, the market for each month showed a pattern of initially rising and then becoming flat. Quotations for foreign wheat were around 1-2 jiao higher for Chicago and slightly lower for Canadian wheat. When the prices opened, sentiment remained high for both near and distant terms. The current month's opening price immediately rose to 6.5 jiao, and the prices for distant months also increased by 3-4 fen compared to the previous day. During the second session, the prices for August, September, and October further increased by 1-2 fen compared to the opening prices due to strong buying interest from inland merchants and price increases by speculators in the market. However, as the mills took advantage of this strong sentiment to gradually sell off positions, the volume was considerable. Therefore, by the third session, the market softened and sentiment turned weak, leading to a decline. After the afternoon opening, the market initially remained stable, but then trading sharply decreased due to scarce buyers. The merchants showed little movement, while there was both buying and selling in futures, and the mills also slightly reduced their positions, causing the market to continue to weaken. The current month saw particularly loose conditions because the mills did not replenish their stocks and the merchants did not withdraw their purchases. As a result, the current month only improved by half a fen, while September decreased by 7.5 li, October improved by 1 fen, November improved by 2.5 li, December remained unchanged, and January improved by 1 fen.

The Quiet and Firm Futures Wheat 222

Yesterday in the futures wheat market, after the morning opening, the market for each month unanimously showed a high and rising trend. Quotations for foreign wheat from both Chicago and Canada had a difference of 1-2 jiao. With the tension in the flour market the previous day and a lively market atmosphere, the asking prices for each month increased invisibly after the opening, improving by 7-9 fen compared to the closing prices of the previous day. However, although the market appeared tight, trading was not very active, mainly because outside speculators were also hesitant to buy. After the afternoon opening, the flour market softened from its high, and buying interest in each session became sluggish, falling back by 2-3 fen from the high prices of the morning session. As a result, the current month improved by 4 fen, September improved by 5 fen, October improved by 7 fen, November improved by 6 fen, and December improved by 7 fen. In the spot wheat market, because the standard has risen and rice prices have also been increasing, high-quality wheat has increased by 6-7 fen, while medium and lower quality wheat remained flat. Shandong Xuzhou Guide wheat opened at 4 yuan and 7 fen, Bengbu wheat at 4 yuan and 5 fen, Yaowan wheat at 4 yuan and 1 fen, Daqiao wheat at 3 yuan and 9.5 jiao, Liuhe wheat at 3 yuan and 9.2 fen, Hankou wheat at 3 yuan and 6.8 fen, and lower quality wheat at 6.5 jiao. Life and Common Sense 229

— Shen Minxing

Among the children, surely some will ask upon seeing the title: "What exactly is common sense?"

Indeed, now I can tell you, common sense is a kind of general knowledge. Its scope is very broad. It is what we humans use to solve all ordinary things and problems in daily life, creating a sound life.

Many people say, "Humans are rational creatures." It can be seen that humans and knowledge cannot be separated. Everything in life depends on knowledge to succeed. A person without abundant knowledge will fail at most things.

Common sense is the entirety of knowledge, the only difference being that it is "broad but not specialized." Therefore, a person lacking common sense will certainly not have a perfect life.

Children, do you want to be a healthy and perfect person? Then you cannot lack common sense. No matter where, no matter when, no matter what happens, as long as common sense exists, you must use sharp eyes to recognize all kinds of new things, creating many new careers. That is so gratifying!

Among children, common sense is undoubtedly the best tool for creating a healthy life, and it is also the most abundant spiritual food!

General Hindenburg 230

— Hanyu

General Hindenburg unfortunately died.

He was the president of Germany, and also a famous general. He could drive out the enemies who invaded his country, and could defend his own land, never losing it.

In the third year of the Republic of China (1914 AD), a great war broke out in Europe. One side was the German and Austrian countries, and the other side was the English, French, and Russian countries. Russia had already invaded several provinces of Germany. At that time, there was a general in Germany who could drive the Russian army out of German territory. This was General Hindenburg.

At the end of the European War, countries around the world went to attack Germany. Of course, although Germany was strong, it could not deal with all the countries in the world. So Germany was failing steadily. But there was a general who guarded his battlements. Until the armistice, no country was able to break through him. This was also General Hindenburg.

General Hindenburg had patriotic enthusiasm, strong will, and great courage. He was a German national hero. We should commemorate him, emulate him, so that China can also have Hindenburg-like figures emerge to drive away our enemies!

How Does a Light Bulb Emit Light? 232

— Zheng

Smart children! You read and write under electric lights every night, how convenient. You should know what an electric light is. How does an electric light emit light?

There is no air inside the bulb of an electric light. How is there no air? It is removed using a special machine that removes air, so some people call it a vacuum.

In the upper part of the bulb, there is a thick piece of glass. Inside the glass are two thicker wires, which are called platinum wires. In the lower part of the bulb, there is a very long carbon filament, which hangs in the middle on a glass pillar like waves. The carbon filament is connected to the platinum wires.

When the electric current passes from the platinum wires to the carbon filament, great resistance occurs. With resistance, light is emitted. If tungsten wire is used instead of carbon filament, the light emitted will be stronger, because the resistance of tungsten wire is greater than that of carbon filament.

The nature of electric current is very dangerous. Touching electric current can cause electric shock and death.

So please pay special attention, children: the switches and plugs of electric lights are very scary and must not be played with.

Tiny Library 233

— Yongqian

The long summer vacation of more than a month is really boring. Mom keeps urging Wen'er to review his books, and Wen'er agrees in his mouth, but in his heart he is 120% uncomfortable.

Coincidentally, this day classmate Xiang'er came to ask him to rent some books to read, and Wen'er thought of setting up a tiny library. Xiang'er agreed, so they went separately to ask the children in the alley and some nearby classmates to participate. The conditions for participation were: write your name on all the books you own and hand them in. They will be returned when the library closes. The benefit is: you can come to Wen'er's house at any time every day to read books.

This day the tiny library opened. Wen'er arranged the books that the members had handed in, read, and looked at, Children, Children's World..., and numbered them and wrote a catalog and posted it on the wall. Everyone elected Wen'er as the president and Xiang'er as the vice president. So from this day on, many people read books. He reads your book, you read other people's books. Many children were introduced by members and brought books to join, and the library became more and more lively, and they also met many new friends and gained a lot of new knowledge during this summer vacation. If they didn't understand something, they asked Wen'er. If Wen'er didn't understand, he asked the public. If anyone knew, they would announce it.

Children, are you willing to organize one? Just invite some nearby children, everyone take out their books, and learn from the tiny library, how beneficial it is!

Fairy Tale (1) 235

(1) The clown said to the four children: There is a cave down the mountain behind us. I want to go in and see what's inside. Do you want to go? (2) Everyone said they were very happy to go and see what was inside. Unexpectedly, as soon as they got to the entrance of the cave, they heard a "peng peng" sound, and everyone was very strange. Mr. Cow and Mrs. Pig 236

— Shi

Mr. Cow finished working in the field, brought back a body of mud, dragged his heavy steps, and slowly walked back. He saw his neighbor Mrs. Pig lying there leisurely, feeding the little pig affectionately. Mr. Cow felt a little unfair in his heart. He thought: I am exactly the same as it, why should I work so hard every day? Leaving in the morning and returning at night, exchanging strength for sweat, exchanging strength for mud, but it only eats and sleeps, growing so fat. So Mr. Cow shouted:

"Lazy good-for-nothing who only eats!"

Mrs. Pig felt that someone was scolding it, so she jumped up and replied:

"What about you?"

"Our generations of descendants have to work before eating. If you don't work, you don't get to eat. Everyone works hard to cultivate, and then they get to eat. There is absolutely no reason to sit and eat." Mr. Cow said sternly.

"You're the stupid one. Our master sends food twice a day. We never work and we get to eat. How happy is this kind of life? You work, eating cold wind in winter and basking in the sun in summer, and you eat the same as us. Isn't this just making trouble for yourself?" Mrs. Pig said triumphantly.

Mr. Cow and Mrs. Pig had a quarrel, but it still didn't lead to any results. Mr. Cow only felt that he was too hard-working.

Later, the New Year came, and the master wanted to use pork to host a banquet, so he killed Mrs. Pig. Mr. Cow rested comfortably for more than ten days during the New Year.

Unity 237

— Rong

The bright red pomegranate flowers have withered, but they leave behind one fruit after another, hanging in the middle of the branches. Under this pomegranate tree is a pile of grass, and ants often walk back and forth in the grass.

One day, a centipede was resting there. The ants were busy looking for food. A small ant happened to pass by and suddenly saw such a large amount of food. It was very happy in its heart, so it went back to the cave to report.

After a while, many ants lined up and walked straight towards the centipede. After a while, just as they were about to prepare to carry the centipede away, the centipede woke up. In its great anger, it used all its strength to deal with the ants, and soon beat them into disarray. Later, because there were more and more ants, they bit it to death, and everyone happily carried the centipede back to the cave.

I feel that those ants were able to bite the strong enemy to death because they had the power of unity. We Chinese people must also learn from the ants, have the power of unity, and jointly deal with the enemy, so that we can not be bullied by them!

Why Do Dogs Stick Their Tongues Out in the Summer? 238

— Qiu Yiting, a fifth-grade student at Shanghai Qianye Elementary School

In the summer, we often see dogs sticking out their tongues. What is the reason for this? Please think about it, everyone!

In general, everything can be studied: we children should especially have an interest in research, like the British inventor Watt, when he was a child, saw the pot lid moving and thought there was an old man with white hair in the pot who was about to jump out. Later, he studied carefully and discovered that the power of steam was very strong, so he invented the steam engine. Now ships, trains, etc., are all derived from Watt's invention.

There is also value in researching why dogs stick out their tongues in the summer. I know the dog's physiology. There are many sweat pores on its tongue, and sweat flows out of the sweat pores, so it has to stick out its tongue. Because its whole body is covered with hair, if the sweat flows out of the skin, won't the hair get wet and sticky? So it has to flow out of the tongue. For example, people also have many sweat pores on their skin, and sweat flows out on the skin, so there is a lot of sweat on the skin in the summer.

Methods of Heat Transfer and Thermos Bottles 239

— Ruoxu

During the summer vacation, in addition to reviewing old books every day to avoid neglecting his studies, Zhifang's father also prescribed a lesson on "Sunday Science Talks," which was taught by his brother every Sunday morning.

On that Sunday, his brother took out a thermos bottle and said:

"There are three methods of heat transfer: one is "conduction," and the other two are "convection" and "radiation." If we hold one end of a wire and put the other end in a fire, our hands gradually feel the heat. This is the heat transmitted by "conduction." If we fill a cup with water and burn the bottom of the cup with fire, we see small bubbles floating up and down (adding some tea leaves to the water will make it even clearer). After a while, the water at the top of the cup also gets hot. This is the heat transmitted by "convection." When we are in the sun or near a stove, we feel hot, which is because "radiation" sends the heat of the sun or the heat of the stove to our bodies."

"The inside of the thermos bottle," said his brother, pointing to the thermos bottle in his hand, "is made of two layers of glass, and there is no air between the glass layers, and a layer of shiny material is applied. Such an arrangement can prevent the three methods of heat transfer, "conduction," "convection," and "radiation," from existing, so if hot things are put inside, the heat will not spread out, and if cold things are put inside, the heat from the outside will not run in to melt it. Therefore, thermos bottles can keep things hot or cold. As for the outer iron shell, it is only used to protect the glass inner lining inside."

Animal Bathing 240

— (Zhushu)

In the summer, don't children often want to avoid bathing? Some children may wonder: why do humans need to bathe, but animals don't?

Let me tell you! Animals also like to bathe. Don't you see the birds in cages often dip their heads into the water and then pull them out? This is their bath. Even cats sometimes stroke their faces with their paws a few times, and dogs also like to raise their hind legs to remove dirt from their bodies. As for horses and donkeys, they roll around on the ground every time they are tired to show that they want to get rid of the fatigue of their muscles and bones, just like humans rubbing a towel on their bodies when bathing, wanting to get rid of fatigue.

Speaking of pigs, they couldn't be dirtier. But they like cleanliness, and they often doze and roll around in the water, as if they couldn't be more comfortable. As for the most obvious animals, such as water buffalo, they are more like friends with water.

Children! Do you like to bathe? Maybe you envy animals for not bathing all day, how carefree! But after you read the paragraph above, what do you think? Don't be greedy for playing anymore, go clean your body!

Lotus Flowers Are Blooming

Dear Children:

The clear fragrance, with the breeze, is sent from the pond to the tip of your nose. Every morning, run to this pond to receive this clear fragrance. Take a deep breath and relieve the depressed mind.

Sitting cross-legged on the ground in the sieve shadow of the willows. The lotus leaves are like plates, with many water droplets on them, rolling around; in an instant, many small beads turn into a shiny one; after a while, they turn into small grains again.

Toads and frogs take the tian tian lotus leaves as cradles, sitting freely in them. When they are happy, they also beat on small membranous drums, making a noise all over the pond.

White and light red lotus flowers emerge from the green leaves, elegant and fragrant, showing their noble character. It is as if they have been baptized by the New Life Movement. We children should be intoxicated in its arms.
